# Skyrim:Camping

## Overview

*This page is about the Creation Club add-on. For camps in Skyrim, see [Skyrim:Camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps").*

| Released | April 5, 2018 |

| Filename | ccqdrsse002-firewood.esl |
| Availability | |

Camping

A Campsite

**Camping** is a [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") that adds a movable campsite for sleeping and cooking in the wilderness. It was released on April 5, 2018 for 300 Creation Credits. The Creation's features work well with [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode").

## Official Summary

:   *Make Skyrim that much more accommodating with this cozy movable campsite, complete with a lean-to for sleeping, campfire for warmth and some cooking, and a new fast travel marker (Creation craftable via Forge)*

## Overview

This Creation adds the ability to set up a campsite out in the wilderness. It consists of a shelter to sleep in, a campfire to [cook](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") a limited number of food items, and a crate to sit on. Once placed, the campsite also gets a map marker which can be used for fast travel. To set up or move your campsite, you will first need to craft [Camping Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Camping_Supplies "Skyrim:Camping Supplies"). This item requires three [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") and one piece of [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather") and can be crafted at any [forge or anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"). Upon setting up camp for the first time, you will be given a brief tutorial message:

:   *"Campsites allow you to rest and stay warm while exploring the wilderness. You can cook a limited number of meals over the campfire. Your campsite is marked on your map so you can locate and fast travel to it later."*

The reference to staying warm refers to the [Warmth](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmth "Skyrim:Warmth")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") mechanic added by the [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") Creation. The Camping Creation is intended to be used in conjunction with Survival Mode, due to the new requirements relating to warmth and sleep which are imposed in that mode. With Survival Mode enabled, the campfire will allow you to warm up by staying near it, although Argonians may need to light a torch as well. It will also allow you to craft a limited number of [hot soups](/wiki/Skyrim:Hot_Soups "Skyrim:Hot Soups") for later use.

This Creation also adds a new [loading screen](/wiki/Skyrim:Loading_Screens "Skyrim:Loading Screens") relating to campsites and a new "Camping" section to the in-game Help menu.

## Content

:   [Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Camping_Items "Skyrim:Camping Items")

    - [Camping Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Camping_Supplies "Skyrim:Camping Supplies")

    Places

    - Campsite

## Notes

- Hot soups can no longer be crafted at a campfire with the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"). Only meals with food that is caught or hunted can be crafted, such as fish and rabbits.
- The [Well Rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Rested "Skyrim:Well Rested") bonus is not granted when sleeping at a campsite.
- Each instance of camping supplies is one use only. They do not return to your inventory upon choosing to break camp.
- In Survival mode, sleeping in your camp will still leave you Drained, as it counts as sleeping outdoors.
- Only one campsite can be set up at a time. You do not need to break camp before creating a new campsite. The old camp will break upon creation of a new campsite.

# Skyrim:Camps

## Overview

Dragon Bridge Overlook

 This page lists **camps**, including [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") camps and [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") camps, in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [Military camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Camps "Skyrim:Military Camps") and [giant camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") are listed on separate pages and use different map marker icons.

:    **[Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A camp east of Thirsk Mead Hall containing Nords exiled from the hall by rieklings. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Bujold%27s+Retreat)
:    **[Dragon Bridge Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Overlook "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Overlook")** — A small Forsworn camp south of Dragon Bridge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragon+Bridge+Overlook)
:    **[Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt")** — A small Forsworn camp and cave south of Mor Khazgur. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Druadach+Redoubt)
:    **[Haknir's Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Shoal "Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small pirate camp north-northwest of Skaal Village. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Haknir%27s+Shoal)
:    **[Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp")** — A small bandit camp and iron mine north of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Halted+Stream+Camp)
:    **[Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire")** — A large Forsworn camp and cave east of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthspire)
:    **[Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge")** — A small bandit camp and iron and corundum mine northwest of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Knifepoint+Ridge)
:    **[Last Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Vigil "Skyrim:Last Vigil")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small camp northeast of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Last+Vigil+%28DB%29)
:    **[Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge")** — A small bandit camp and cave west-southwest of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Robber%27s+Gorge)
:    **[Serpent's Bluff Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpent%27s_Bluff_Redoubt "Skyrim:Serpent's Bluff Redoubt")** — A small Forsworn camp and ruin southwest of Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Serpent%27s+Bluff+Redoubt)

## Notes

- You can set up your own **[campsite](/wiki/Skyrim:Campsite "Skyrim:Campsite")** with the [Camping](/wiki/Skyrim:Camping "Skyrim:Camping") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed. The campsite adds a fast travel marker to your map, although you can only have one campsite set up at a time.

# Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall

## Overview

|  |  |  |

Candlehearth Hall

**Candlehearth Hall** is a large [tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") in the center of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

A brief history from the tavern's owner, [Elda Early-Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Elda_Early-Dawn "Skyrim:Elda Early-Dawn"), reveals the building was originally home to a great warrior named Vundheim from the early [Fourth Era](/wiki/Lore:Fourth_Era "Lore:Fourth Era"). When he died in [4E 38](/wiki/Lore:Fourth_Era#4E_38 "Lore:Fourth Era") his son, Deroct, lit a candle above the hearth in his honor. Since that day, the candle still burns and as such the inn owes its name to this phenomenon.

It is a popular destination for many of the city's folk for beverages and the performances from the bards. [Nils](/wiki/Skyrim:Nils "Skyrim:Nils") serves as cook, but will take over running the inn if Elda dies. It consists of one area, *[Candlehearth Hall](#Candlehearth_Hall)*.

## Residents

| Residents |

| [Adonato Leotelli](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato_Leotelli "Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli")  [Captain Lonely-Gale](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Lonely-Gale "Skyrim:Captain Lonely-Gale")  [Durian](/wiki/Skyrim:Durian "Skyrim:Durian") \*\*\*  [Elda Early-Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Elda_Early-Dawn "Skyrim:Elda Early-Dawn") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Luaffyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Luaffyn "Skyrim:Luaffyn")  [Nils](/wiki/Skyrim:Nils "Skyrim:Nils") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") \*  [Rolff Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Rolff_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Rolff Stone-Fist")  [Stenvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Stenvar "Skyrim:Stenvar") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Stormcloak Courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Courier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Courier") †  [Susanna the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Susanna_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Susanna the Wicked")  [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") \*\*  [Tekla](/wiki/Skyrim:Tekla "Skyrim:Tekla") \*\* |

## Related Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

## Candlehearth Hall

The top floor with the namesake candle above the hearth

Candlehearth Hall is divided into two stories, a ground floor and a top floor. The ground floor functions as a taproom and has proprietor [Elda Early-Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Elda_Early-Dawn "Skyrim:Elda Early-Dawn") behind her counter, at times chatting with the regulars. The second floor is spacious and consists of one huge room with several tables where the regulars can enjoy their drinks and the [performances](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances") from the bard, [Luaffyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Luaffyn "Skyrim:Luaffyn").

The top floor consists of one large room and is where most of the regulars gather during the day. Luaffyn stands in the southwestern corner, next to the ladder leading down to the kitchen. In front of her is the trademark hearth and the eternally burning candle. Facing the hearth are three chairs accompanied by tables with some assorted food, two [eidar cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), some [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), one of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). On the other side of the hearth is another table with some [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and one of alto wine. Adjacent to the stairs leading down to the bar is an exit to Windhelm and a table with an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"). In the southeastern corner, [Stenvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Stenvar "Skyrim:Stenvar") sits around the clock, ready to be hired as a mercenary for 500 gold. The table in front of him has a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"). In the adjacent corner is the table where local author and potential [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")-giver [Adonato Leotelli](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato_Leotelli "Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli") often sits when he writes his tales of heroism. His table has a slice of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), and a bottle of Nord mead.

The ground floor

The ground floor has two entrances next to each other, both of them located adjacent to the main gate of Windhelm. Both entrances open to the sight of Elda behind her bar on the left, the guestrooms and kitchens down the hallway in front, and the stairs leading to the second floor on the right. A single bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") stands on the bar, while Elda hides several items underneath it, including a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and ten [gold coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold#Currency "Skyrim:Gold"). On the shelves behind her sit a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), along with several more alcoholic beverages, including four bottles of alto wine, two bottles of regular wine, and seven bottles of Nord mead.

Down the hallway are four rooms, three of which have beds while the fourth is the kitchen and has a ladder leading up to the second floor. [The Crimson Dirks, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v4 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v4")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale") can be found on a table in the hallway. The first room to the right is where [Nils](/wiki/Skyrim:Nils "Skyrim:Nils") sleeps between 2am and 8am. Along the western wall is a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") on the floor, while a small dinner table in the northwestern corner holds a bottle of Nord mead, some baked potatoes, and a honey nut treat. The cupboard in the adjacent corner holds clutter and the shelves above contain a bottle of wine, a copy of the [quest-related](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)") book *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*. The southeastern corner has an end table with clutter and a large food sack along with it. Near the door is a set of shelves with three food sacks and the tavern's [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger").

The room for rent

The first room on the left is the room you can rent for 10 gold. Just inside the door is a dresser with [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") and a bit of food on top: a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). In the corner next to the dresser is a set of shelves with a food sack, a potion of healing, a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"). Next up is a wardrobe with more clothes and the bed. At the foot of the bed is an end table with clutter and a bottle of wine on top.

The second room on the left is reserved for the [Stormcloak courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Courier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Courier") during the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") quest [A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)"), if you side with the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). Save for a few items, the room is almost completely empty. The door opens to a wardrobe with clothing, and, along the northern wall, more clothing in a dresser and a bottle of wine. The owned bed stands in the southeastern corner.

The kitchen is where [Nils](/wiki/Skyrim:Nils "Skyrim:Nils") cooks every day between 4pm and 10pm and consists of a huge amount of different foodstuffs and a ladder to the second floor. In the southeastern corner is a set of shelves and a cupboard, separated by two large food sacks, and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") on the floor. The shelves on the right contain three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a goat cheese wedge, a slice of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), two salt piles, a sample of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), a bottle of alto wine, and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). The cupboard contains clutter but has several items on the shelves above, including a food sack, a [chef's hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat"), a bottle of Nord mead, a bottle of wine, a chunk of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a bottle of alto wine, and an apprentice-locked non-respawning [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), which contains random items. Following the wall towards the [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), next is a small table with more food, an apple pie, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg") and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Above the table hangs some game, specifically two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), along with two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid") and a bouquet of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"). Near the fireplace, underneath the kettles sit three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") and, in a cast iron pot in the northwestern corner, a slice of bread. In the alcove leading to the ladder are four food sacks and a small table with even more food, a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a bottle of Nord mead, a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), four heads of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and three carrots.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 4 | [Honningbrew Meads](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- If Elda dies and Nils takes over, he will not stand behind the counter. You can, however, acquire his innkeeper services around the clock. See [this article](/wiki/Skyrim:Nils "Skyrim:Nils") for his schedule.
- Fighting [Rolff Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Rolff_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Rolff Stone-Fist") anywhere in the city makes low-level items free to take, but all the beds are still owned until you pay for the room.
- All cupboards, dressers, and end tables in the location are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- The candle above the fireplace will spill blood when attacked as if it were an NPC. This is actually caused by an erroneous havok material on the chimney itself; the chimney is what is being struck. The candle itself is a generic static object.
- During the [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") or immediately thereafter, if you enter Candlehearth Hall through the right entrance the other door will have an expert lock needed to get out. Re-entering Candlehearth Hall from the right entrance again locks the door from the inside and will still give XP. **?**
- The innkeeper's vendor chest here doesn't always stock bread despite Elda saying she sells it consistently.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.

Captain Aldis

Roggvir's execution

**Captain Aldis** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") captain in the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in charge of the [Solitude guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard"). When you first arrive in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), he is personally overseeing the execution of [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir"). He can normally be found pacing the courtyard of [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour"). If you side with the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), he will disappear from the game entirely at the beginning of the [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude").

Aldis follows a rigorous schedule, supervising the training of Imperial soldiers in the Castle Dour courtyard from 8am until 8pm each day, then returning to the castle to sleep from 8pm to 8am the next morning.

He wears [Solitude guard's armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard%27s_Armor "Skyrim:Solitude Guard's Armor"), with [Imperial bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Bracers") and matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Boots"). He carries a [Solitude guard's shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Solitude Guard's Shield"), an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), an [Imperial bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow"), and ten [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow").

## Related Quests

- **[For the Good of Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:For_the_Good_of_Morthal "Skyrim:For the Good of Morthal")**: Deliver a letter to Captain Aldis in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
- **[No News is Good News](/wiki/Skyrim:No_News_is_Good_News "Skyrim:No News is Good News")**: Find out about the fate of [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard")'s daughter from Captain Aldis.
- **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Rare Gifts

While Aldis is supervising the training of Imperial soldiers, you can ask him if he is with the Legion:

:   **Are you with the Legion?**
:   *"That I am. Train the recruits. Turn boys into men. That sort of thing. Thinking of asking the General for some training books. Give the soldiers something to do while they're on rest. Something besides drinking. Ever seen a book called 'The Mirror'? We used to hand it out to boys looking to learn basic shield work."*

:   :   **That's too bad.**
    :   *"Be glad you're not training under me with that mouth of yours.*"

:   :   **If I find a copy, I'll bring it to you.**
    :   *"Good on you."*

If you find [the book](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mirror "Skyrim:The Mirror") and return it to Aldis:

:   **I found that book you wanted.**
:   *"Good. I'll see if I can get some copies made for the men. Here, something for your trouble. The Legion thanks you."*

### No News is Good News

During the quest [No News Is Good News](/wiki/Skyrim:No_News_is_Good_News "Skyrim:No News is Good News"), you are tasked with obtaining information from Aldis about [Angeline Morrard's](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard") daughter:

:   **Captain, Angela *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* sent me to ask about her daughter.**
:   *"Generally posting information is need to know only."*

You then have the following options:

| Player Choice | Aldis' Response |
| --- | --- |
| **"I think Angela *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* needs to know."**  *(Persuade)* | **Passed:** *"I... I've been trying to find the time and place to let her know."* **Failed:** *"I'm sorry, I can't help you."* |
| **"Well, I'm making it "need to know."**  *(Intimidate)* | **Passed:** *"If you want to know that bad then fine."* **Failed:** *"I'm afraid that kind of thing doesn't work on Captains in the Imperial Army."* |
| **"Fine. If that's the way you want it."** | **Failed:** *"That's the way it is."* |
| **"Tell me about her daughter. That's an order, Captain."** | **Passed:** *"Yes, Sir. Although I'm not sure you'll be happy to know."* |

In any instance in which you pass, he will respond with:

:   *"Her daughter was sent to Whiterun, the skirmishes there have been violent. The whiterun*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *legate, he needed to know the Stormcloak positions. He sent out a party to scout the area. They happened upon a large force... I'm told none of them made it back. Private Morrard... Angela*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*'s daughter was in that scouting party. She needs to be told."*

### For the Good of Morthal

During the quest [For the Good of Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:For_the_Good_of_Morthal "Skyrim:For the Good of Morthal"), you are tasked with delivering a letter from [Gorm](/wiki/Skyrim:Gorm "Skyrim:Gorm") to Aldis:

:   **I have a letter for you.**
:   *"For me? From whom?"*
:   **It's from Gorm, in Morthal.**
:   *"Well now, that is something. Hand it over, please.*"

He will then read the letter, and continue, saying:

:   *"Oh, no. I hadn't heard from Gorm for a while, so I'd hoped he'd given up on his little scheme. The last time we'd discussed this issue was before this damnable war broke out. Things were different then. Now, what's he's asking, it's just impossible. Even if it worked, the questions and accusations it would cause... Well, I'll take it under advisement. Thank you."*

## Dialogue

When spoken to directly you can ask him questions:

:   **You were the one presiding over the execution.**
:   *"Not my finest hour. Roggvir was a fine and honorable man."*

:   :   **So you think what he did was right?**
    :   '*No. I think he was entirely wrong. Roggvir's execution was justified and necessary. Being honorable might make you a good man, but it doesn't make you right. Be a better world if it did."*

:   :   **How could you execute a fine and honorable man?**
    :   *"Sometimes you just do what needs to be done. You don't have to hate a man to kill him. Though, admittedly... it helps."*

If you approach him in Stormcloak armor, he will say:

:   *"What do you think you're doing, walking around dressed like a damn Stormcloak traitor?"*

:   :   **Sorry, I didn't mean anything by it.**
    :   *"Well. I'll let it slide this time. But you'd be smart to take that off. Someone might get the wrong idea."*

:   :   **I'm a proud supporter of Ulfric Stormcloak. What of it?**
    :   *"Is that right? Here's how the Legion deals with rebel scum like you."*

A 40 gold bounty will then be added to Haafingar and Aldis and any nearby Imperial Legion soldiers will attack you.

While he is training guards in the courtyard of Castle Dour, he may give some instructions to his fellow men, such as:

:   *"Concentrate. The battlefield is full of distractions. Ignore them! Focus on your targets."*
:   *"Come on, now! I want those arrows dead center! The lives of your fellow soldiers are counting on it."*
:   *"Some day soon, you will all see battle. And what you do here, today, may well save your lives!"*

If you ask Aldis how the training is going:

:   **How goes the training?**
:   *"Their aim could be steadier, but they're battle ready."*
:   **Even if that battle is with a dragon?**
:   *"Can any man hope to be ready for a dragon? I can but hone their skills and harden their hearts. The rest is up to the gods."* **or** *"You're the Dragonborn aren't you? I'm sort of hoping you're going to fight the dragons for us. A normal man is no match for a dragon."*

After finishing speaking with him, Aldis can say:

:   *"Keep my men in your prayers. They'll need them if they don't shape up."*
:   *"Stay strong. The Eight willing, we'll win this war."*

### Unused

Captain Aldis has some unused dialogue related to a removed portion of the quest "[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")".

Originally, after the [Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Icerunner "Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner") had ran aground, Aldis would meet up with you on the beach and help you take down the bandits.

:   *"You're the one Mazzaka*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *described to me."*

:   **Who are you?**
:   *"I'm Captain Aldis. I'm here to help you take down these bandits."*

:   **Just you?**
:   *"We're stretched thin in Solitude, and I don't expect these bandits to be much challenge. Are you ready?"*

:   **Let's take them out.**
:   *"With pleasure."*

Aldis apparently would not be present during the fight with [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja"). The fight was also different, as you could either spare or kill her. If you killed her, you would report this to Aldis:

:   **Looks like Deeja won't be bothering us again.**
:   *"Good riddance."*

But, if she was left alive, then you would request for her to be imprisoned:

:   **Deeja will need to be locked up.**
:   *"I'll take care of it."*

The lines for both of these outcomes are strangely attached to [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") and only recorded in his voice type.

After the Icerunner had been cleared out, Aldis would say:

:   *"I've been away from Solitude for as long as I can. But if you decide to finish these bandits off, you'll be rewarded for your efforts."*

You could actually report your success to Aldis after dealing with Jaree and his crew:

:   **I dealt with the rest of the bandits.**
:   *"It's appreciated. The captains around here will have one less thing to worry about. Here's your reward.*"

You would ultimately receive 200 gold from Aldis for doing this task.

## Conversations

During Roggvir's execution:

:   **[Svari](/wiki/Skyrim:Svari "Skyrim:Svari")**: *"They can't hurt uncle Roggvir. Tell them he didn't do it."*
:   **Captain Aldis**: *"Positions."*
:   **[Addvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar "Skyrim:Addvar")**: *"Svari, you need to go home. Go home and stay there until your mother comes."*
:   **[Vivienne Onis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis")**: *"You should tell her that her uncle is scum that betrayed his High King. Best she know now, Addvar."*
:   **Addvar**: *"You're all heart, Vivienne."*
:   **Captain Aldis**: *"Roggvir. You helped Ulfric Stormcloak escape this city after he murdered High King Torygg. By opening that gate for Ulfric you betrayed the people of Solitude."*
:   **[Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand")**: *"Traitor!"*
:   **[Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius")**: *"He doesn't deserve to speak!"*
:   **Roggvir**: *"There was no murder! Ulfric challenged Torygg. He beat the High King in fair combat."*
:   **Roggvir**: *"Such as our way! Such as the ancient custom of Skyrim, and all Nords!"*
:   **[Jala](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala "Skyrim:Jala")**: *"Booooo."'*
:   **Sorex Vinius**: *"Booooo."*
:   **Taarie**: *"Booooo."*
:   **Roggvir**: *"On this day... I go to Sovngarde."*

## Bugs

- If you finish the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") quest [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude"), Aldis will no longer be part of the city. Consequently any quests involving him that have been started will point to a blank ground, where Aldis previously stood.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - There is no solution other than entering the appropriate commands on the PC to finish the quests. It is therefore recommended to finish any quests related to Aldis before starting the Battle for Solitude.
- Captain Aldis will incorrectly refer to female characters as "sir" when he is asked about Angeline's daughter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- You can order Captain Aldis to give you the information on Angeline's daughter even if you're not of the proper rank in the Imperial Legion, or if you're not a member of the Legion at all.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Captain Aquilius

**Captain Aquilius** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") who only appears during [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers") as you leave [Calcelmo's Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo%27s_Tower "Skyrim:Calcelmo's Tower") after copying the tablet. If [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar") is still alive, he will instruct Aquilius to search the building.

He wears [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor") if you are below level 18, and [steel plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor") if you are above. He carries a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") if you are below level 6 and a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield") if you are above. In addition, he wields a leveled one-handed weapon and carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo%27s_Laboratory_Key "Skyrim:Calcelmo's Laboratory Key") to [Calcelmo's Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep#Calcelmo.27s_Laboratory "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum_Key "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum Key") to the [Dwemer Museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep#Dwemer_Museum "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), and leveled amount of gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers")**: Help translate [Gallus's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal").

### Hard Answers

When you make a rubbing of Calcelmo's Stone, Aicantar will burst into the room with his guards and Captain Aquilius:

:   **Aicantar**: *"Accidents like this just don't happen. Someone is trying to sabotage my uncle's research."*
:   **Aquilius**: *"I...all right. If there is a thief, he won't leave this tower alive. But shouldn't we inform Master Calcelmo?"*
:   **Aicantar**: *"I'll deal with my uncle. Just...go! Scour this place from top to bottom!"*
:   **Aquilius**: *"All right men, spread out and search the tower. No telling who - or what - we're dealing with here."*

Captain Avidius

**Captain Avidius** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_(class) "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus (class)") who is found on [The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah") during the quest [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"). He wears [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006ff45 "Skyrim:Clothes") with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots") and is armed with an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"). He carries the [Katariah Master Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Katariah_Master_Key "Skyrim:Katariah Master Key"), along with two leveled potions of [restore health](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health") and at least 25 gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.

## Overview

| Captain Hargar (RefID: 0002C486) | | | |

| Level | Radiant (1-25) | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0002C486 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001E38B |
| Other Information | | | |

| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 70-246 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, **[Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed")**, [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleCommonerAccented](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCommonerAccented "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCommonerAccented") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [MS07BanditFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MS07BanditFaction "Skyrim:MS07BanditFaction") | | |

Captain Hargar

**Captain Hargar** is the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") leader of the [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder") residing in the caved-in [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto"). He wears [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor") with matching [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"). He wields a leveled [two-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:Two-Handed Weapons") that can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality, and carries a small amount of gold.

He is working together with [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") and his sister [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja") on some big raid [scheme](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"). When you track down the former to the grotto during the related quest, Hargar will try and protect his ally. Apparently, Hargar was locked up inside of the [Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon") up until recently, when he escaped. Solitude's executioner, [Ahtar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahtar "Skyrim:Ahtar") will send you to kill him during his [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.

## Notes

- Hargar's [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hargar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hargar's Journal") can be found on the table at the uppermost level of the wooden tower in Broken Oar Grotto, and will inform you of some hidden treasure nearby. The key to the master-locked chest can be pickpocketed from him or looted off his corpse after he's killed.
- It is advisable to complete Ahtar's quest before any other quests in Broken Oar Grotto, as killing Captain Hargar will render that quest inaccessible, thus making it difficult to ever use Ahtar as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

Captain Lonely-Gale

**Captain Lonely-Gale** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") living in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He's a retired sailor, and a pretty well-known face around Windhelm. He's also a widower, which has attracted the unwanted attention of local woman [Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano"). He was supposed to become [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")'s steward after Ulfric is deposed, but doesn't due to a [bug](#Bugs).

The retired captain enjoys a rather relaxed life in Windhelm, although he never sleeps, spending most of his time in Candlehearth Hall. He does leave to browse the market stalls for 4 hours at 8am, followed immediately by 6 hours of wandering the city.

His outfit consists of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000f8715 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000cee82 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He is also equipped with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") and carries around a selection of [rich class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When the captain greets you, he almost always refers to his past:

:   *"I made my fortune as a sea captain, but now I'm retired."*
:   *"The townsfolk call me "captain" because I used to be a sailor."*
:   *"I lost my family years ago. Truth is, I don't really know what keeps me going."*

However, should [Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano") still be alive, he might assume you were sent by her:

:   *"Did Viola send you to bother me?"*

He also seems very knowledgeable of the city, and has a lot of topics regarding it. For example, you could ask him about what there is to do:

:   **What's there to do in the city?**
:   *"If you're looking to pass the time, you can give [Calixto](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium") a few septims and gawk at whater*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *oddity he's come across lately. If you're need of goods, there's a market. If it's a soft bed and a hot meal you're after, there's [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall")."*

You can also ask him about the city's prominent citizens:

:   **Who are the prominent citizens in Windhelm?**
:   *"There's an author named [Adonato](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato_Leotelli "Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli") staying at the inn. He's published a few works of historical fiction. The clans [Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") and [Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") see most of the gold that passes through the city. And obviously you have [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") and future High King. Oh, and that busybody Viola Giordano. She's got her nose in everyone's business, which I guess is one way of being prominent."*

You can also talk about the ongoing [murders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice"):

:   **Folk are talking about murders.**
:   *"Terrible shame, that. Seems we have a killer on the loose here in Windhelm. He's claimed three victims that I know of, though maybe there's more that haven't been found yet. All lovely young ladies*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, too. Let's hope the guards find that demon soon, and introduce him to the headsman's axe."*

It's also possible to ask about his title:

:   **What kind of captain are you?**
:   *"Well, nothing. At least not any more. Folk just call me that because of what I used to do. I was a sailor for many a year. I made my coin as a trader and in time, I bought my own ship. When I retired here in Windhelm, most folk already knew me as Captain Lonely-Gale, and the name just stuck."*

When exiting conversations, his farewells may reflect his past once more:

:   *"Fair winds and calm seas. That's an old sailor's parting."*
:   *"It was a pleasure to talk to someone so interesting."*

## Conversations

At the marketplace, Lonely-Gale might converse with shady vendor [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye"):

:   **Niranye**: *"Captain Lonely-Gale, it's always a pleasure to see you. In fact, I'm glad you're here. There's something I'd like to ask you."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"A pleasure to see you as well, Niranye. What can I do for you?"*
:   **Niranye**: *"I was wondering if you still had many associates in the shipping profession. I have a business proposition for any sailors who might be looking to make a few extra septims."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"If that business proposition includes smuggling, forget it. The sailors I know are plenty good at finding trouble without any help from you."*
:   **Niranye**: *"You're such a wet blanket, captain. Can't a girl have a little fun from time to time?"*

Inside [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"), he may also speak with the innkeeper, [Elda Early-Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Elda_Early-Dawn "Skyrim:Elda Early-Dawn"):

:   **Elda**: *"Captain, have you heard these stories of dragons?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Elda, you know better than to believe every idiot traveler that wanders through."*
:   **Elda**: *"But they're saying that one of them freed Ulfric... that he's in league with them."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Think about how ridiculous that sounds. Come now."*

:   **Elda**: *"So what's the news on the street, Captain?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"The dark elves are uneasy. There's a killer on the streets. And Viola Giordano won't leave me alone."*
:   **Elda**: *"How would you like a drink?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Very much so."*
:   **Elda**: *"Coming right up."*

He may also be spoken to by Viola Giordano if she crosses his path while walking through the streets:

:   **Viola**: *"Captain, captain!"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"What is it now, Viola?"*
:   **Viola**: *"Did you notice that the snow settles in a different direction near the murder sites?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Don't you think all your tramping around there investigating might have something to do with it?"*
:   **Viola**: *"I... well. Perhaps. But still! It's curious."*

:   **Viola**: *"Captain Lonely-Gale! I've been looking for you everywhere!"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"And now you've found me. Can I help you?"*
:   **Viola**: *"Have you thought about my invitation?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"I've thought about it, but I'm not sure it's such a good idea."*
:   **Viola**: *"Oh, I see. Is it still too soon?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Yes, I think that must be it. My wife hasn't been gone that long, after all. Ask me again on another day."*
:   **Viola**: *"I'm sorry to be such a bother. We'll talk another time."*

:   **Viola**: *"Do you think those dark elves had anything to do with the murders? The attacks all happened at night, after all."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Viola, dark elves sleep just like the rest of us."*
:   **Viola**: *"You wouldn't think it from the racket that Cornerclub makes."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"I'm sure the guards have the matter well in hand. Now, if you'll excuse me."*

:   **Viola**: *"Hello, captain! Can you spare a moment? I heard something the other day that I wanted to share with you."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"What did you hear?"*
:   **Viola**: *"It was an old Nord proverb. It said, the best way to get over the loss of a lover is to find a new one."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"I didn't lose a lover, Viola, I lost my wife. It's not the same thing."*
:   **Viola**: *"Well, if it works in the one case, why not the other? Don't you want to at least give it a try?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"No, I really don't. It'll be a while before I'm ready for that. I'll be on my way now."*

## Unused Conversations

Originally, a scene was also meant to play out between Lonely-Gale and Ambarys Rendar when you entered the city for the first time, but it never plays in the final game. It seems that Lonely-Gale originally played the role of Windhelm's guard captain:

:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"If anything actually happens, call a guard."*
:   **Ambarys**: *"If the guards in the Gray Quarter weren't a bunch of n'wahs, I wouldn't be here talking to you."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"My men have their orders. But it's a big city and there's a war on. Plus these murders. A few dark elves getting shoved around doesn't really amount to much."*
:   **Ambarys**: *"Typical Nord. Beard for brains."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Watch that tongue, Rendar, or your whole lot could be down with the Argonians hauling ballast by tomorrow."*

Two more scenes exist which had Lonely-Gale function as a guard captain, once again, these go unused. They imply that he was at one point meant to head to the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") in order to report to [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") himself:

:   **Ulfric**: *"Captain, I've been receiving complaints about this Giordano woman."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Yes, sir. I've been trying to quiet her, but she's insistent. She thinks she can find out who's been killing the women..."*
:   **Ulfric**: *"I don't care if she can find a living dwarf -- I can't have her stirring up trouble. We have enough problems as it is."*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Yes, sir. I'll try to contain her."*
:   **Ulfric**: *"See that you do. I will not let Windhelm descend into chaos over a few overactive imaginations."*

:   **Ulfric**: *"What's the current spirit among the dark elves?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"As restless as ever, sir, but I don't see them taking any kind of incendiary action. Not soon, anyway."*
:   **Ulfric**: *"Well that much is good. Let's finish this first war before starting the next one, eh?"*
:   **Lonely-Gale**: *"Um... yes, of course, sir."*
:   **Ulfric**: *"Carry on, Lonely-Gale. And loosen yourself a bit."*

## Unused Dialogue

As steward, Captain Lonely-Gale would have had new dialogue, which can never be heard in the base game. He could have been asked about the aftermath of the war:

:   **Is the war really over?**
:   *"I wish I could say that it was, but it's not that simple. Many Stormcloaks will fight until they die, because they still believe they're fighting for Skyrim's freedom. But without Ulfric, the movement will wither and die. It's only a matter of time.*"

It would have also been possible to ask him about the city's history:

:   **Tell me about the city's history.**
:   *"Windhelm is one of the oldest human cities in Tamriel. In fact, it was the capital of the First Empire, which was founded by Ysgramor. The Palace of the Kings in which you now stand is one of the last buildings that remain from that era. Long ago, the Empire used the city to garrison troops who guarded the passes to Morrowind. And now, thanks to you, the city is back under the Empire's banner."*

You could also ask him why he was chosen as steward:

:   **Why did Brunwulf choose you to be Steward?**
:   *"Well, a few reasons come to mind. In my days as a riverboat captain, I was known to run a tight ship. That, and I made my fortune by knowing when to spend my septims and when not to. I can't stand waste."*

In the game's DialogueViews files, an early version of Lonely-Gale's **What's there do in the city?** response can also be found:

:   *"If you're looking to pass the time, you can give Calixto a few septims and gawk at whater*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *oddity he's come across lately. Fight in the Pit if you've got the mettle. Wager on the fights if you don't. If you're need of goods, there's a market. If it's a soft bed and a hot meal you're after, there's Candlehearth Inn."* These lines make mention of The Pit, Windhelm's removed arena, and also use an earlier name for Candlehearth Hall.

## Notes

- In addition to the scenes mentioned above, there are some other internal references to Lonely-Gale being a guard captain, such as him being placed inside of the Palace, as well as a scene between [Adisla](/wiki/Skyrim:Adisla "Skyrim:Adisla") and [Belyn Hlaalu](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu") that still takes place in the final game, where he is still referred to as such.

## Bugs

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), he belongs to the faction [WindhelmSteward](/wiki/Skyrim:WindhelmSteward "Skyrim:WindhelmSteward") and has some dialogue which suggests he was supposed to become [Brunwulf Free-Winter's](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter") [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") if the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") gained Windhelm, but [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif") remains the steward in the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") regardless.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - If the Unofficial Patch cannot fix this, using console commands `addfac 0003662A` to add him back to the Ruling Government should make him steward again. He will therefore give you the option to buy property and decorate it.
- He still speaks about Ulfric being a prominent citizen of Windhelm even after Ulfric is dead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- He still speaks about the murders after [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") is finshed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- His other dialogue about the prominent citizens of Windhelm will also not change if any of the others he mentions are dead. **?**

Captain Valmir disguised as a Stormcloak officer

**Captain Valmir** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") who claims to be an officer of either the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") or the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") depending on which faction you have joined. He is found at the campsite in the courtyard of the ruined fortress of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost"). He asks for your help when you encounter him; speaking with him begins the quest.

When disguised as an Imperial officer, Valmir wears a full set of [Imperial light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor") and wields an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"). When disguised as a Stormcloak officer, he wears a full set of [Stormcloak officer armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Armor "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Armor") and wields a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") which may be up to [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel") in quality. In both cases, he also carries a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and the [key to the entrance of Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost_Entrance_Key "Skyrim:Forelhost Entrance Key").

Captain Valmir knows the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spell [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"), and the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") spell [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing").

## Related Quests

- **[Siege on the Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Siege_on_the_Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult")**: Enter the ruins of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") and defeat [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)") to recover his mask for Captain Valmir.

## Quest-Related Events

If approached he will say:

:   *"You there! As an officer of the Imperial Legion, I require your assistance to complete my mission."*
:   **What mission?**
:   *"The General has sent me to obtain a powerful weapon for the war effort. This was the last great bastion of the Dragon Cult, and their leader's mask was reported to be quite powerful."*

:   :   **General Tullius never mentioned you...**
    :   *"Oh... well... of course they'd disavow all knowledge... spies are everywhere."*

        :   **...**
        :   *"Are you going to help me with my mission? I need someone very capable."*

:   :   **What can you tell me about Forelhost?**
    :   *"It seems that after the strength of the Cult was broken in the Dragon War a last contingent came here to create a stronghold and regroup. King Harald's forces crushed stragglers here the during the First Era and it has been haunted ever since, but the specifics of the siege are unclear."*

:   :   **What can you tell me about the Dragon Cult?**
    :   *"They were among the first men to arrive from Atmora and they worshipped certain animals as avatars of the Gods; Dragons being foremost. And for their bloody sacrifices, the Dragons gifted their priests with terrible power. But their cruelty was too great for men to bear, and they rose up in what would be called the Dragon War and the Cult swept from the land."*

:   :   **If it will help the cause...**
    :   *"Very good."*

If approached again:

:   *"What are you waiting for? Get in there and find that mask."*

:   :   **I haven't found the mask yet.**
    :   *"Well then, what are you waiting for? Get in there and earn your pay."*

:   :   **Why aren't you going in there?**
    :   *"Me? No, I'm too important to the war effort to risk life and limb in there... Besides, that's what I'm paying you for."*

:   :   **I've found the journal of Skorm Snow-Strider.**
    :   *"And what? You couldn't read it yourself? Fine, give it here a moment."*

He will then read the journal:

:   *"Let's see... found the Dragon Cult... laid siege... people already dead... poisoned themselves... blah, blah, blah... ah! Here it is! So the Dragon Cult poisoned their own well, which explains the ghosts. However, Skorm thought the well was the key to entering the inner areas. That all happened in the First Era, so the well should be clear of poison by now. It says the key to the well is likely somewhere in the crypt."*

When you exit Forelhost you will see him speaking to an Imperial or Stormcloak soldier depending on your allegiance:

:   **Captain Valmir:** *"The research I've done seems to indicate that Skorm Snow-Strider left part of his journal here after laying siege. I believe it should indicate how to enter the blocked off sections of the stronghold. I should warn you, Forelhost is quite haunted, but I'm sure you can handle it. Return to me here once you've obtained the staff."*
:   **Imperial Soldier:** *"Wait, it's haunted? I don't like ghosts... let me think about this for a minute... Wait... who in the blazes is this?"*
:   **Captain Valmir:** *"Oh! Um, he he... Hold on... I... I can explain..."*
:   **Imperial Soldier:** *"Valmir, you rat. You're not a soldier at all! Must be one of the Thalmor!"*

:   **Captain Valmir:** *"The research I've done seems to indicate that Skorm Snow-Strider left part of his journal here after laying siege. I believe it should indicate how to enter the blocked off sections of the stronghold. I should warn you, Forelhost is quite haunted, but I'm sure you can handle it. Return to me here once you've obtained the staff."*
:   **Stormcloak Soldier:** *"Wait, it's haunted? I don't like ghosts... let me think about this for a minute... Wait... who in the blazes is this?"*
:   **Captain Valmir:** *"Oh! Um, he he... Hold on... I... I can explain..."*

You will then have to kill both Valmir and the soldier.

## Notes

- Before you enter Forelhost proper for the [Siege on the Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Siege_on_the_Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult") quest, you can pickpocket [Valmir's Orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Valmir%27s_Orders "Skyrim:Valmir's Orders") from him, which reveal that he was actually an agent sent to retrieve a [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(item) "Skyrim:Rahgot (item)") and return it to [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian"). Killing him at that stage of the quest counts as a [murder](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime").
- If you have yet to join either faction in the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") questline by the time you meet Valmir, his disguise of choice will depend on whether you followed the Stormcloak soldier [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") or the Imperial soldier [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") during the quest [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound").
