| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |
| # of [Grindstones](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") | 1 |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |
| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Escape](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Escape") Escape |

Castle Dour, headquarters of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")

**Castle Dour** is a large [fortress](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") which acts as the headquarters of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and residence of the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim").

The exterior of Castle Dour

Castle Dour is separated from the rest of Solitude by high stone walls, with two gateways allowing entry. One gateway is on the southwest side and leads to the Wells District of Solitude, while the other gateway is on the southeast side and leads to the Avenues District, as well as the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"). There are three zones: *[Castle Dour](#Castle_Dour)*, *[Castle Dour Dungeon](#Castle_Dour_Dungeon)*, and *[Emperor's Tower](#Castle_Dour.2C_Emperor.27s_Tower)*.

## Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | Soldiers by rank\* | | --- | | [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius")  [Legate Adventus Caesennius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Adventus_Caesennius "Skyrim:Legate Adventus Caesennius")  [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke")  [Istar Cairn-Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Istar_Cairn-Breaker "Skyrim:Istar Cairn-Breaker")  [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") | | | Others | | --- | | [Gianna](/wiki/Skyrim:Gianna "Skyrim:Gianna") (cook)  [Kevon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kevon "Skyrim:Kevon")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") (dead)  [Solitude Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard") (guards)  [Bjartur](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjartur "Skyrim:Bjartur") (prisoner) | |

\* These NPCs are mutually exclusive; after [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") Tullius, Rikke, Aldis and Adventus will be gone, and Istar will be present.

## Related Quests

- **[Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude")**: Conquer the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [capital](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and free Skyrim from the Empire! ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Battle of the Champions](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_the_Champions "Skyrim:Battle of the Champions")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions"): A battle between two [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") champions is about to begin.
- **[Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death")**: Assassinate [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") at her own wedding.
- **[Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail"): Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").
- **[Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion")**: Prove yourself worthy to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire")**: Attempt to assassinate the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") while disguised as the [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet "Skyrim:Gourmet").
- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

### Exterior

Inside the walls is the courtyard where [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") trains the [Solitude guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard") in archery and swordsmanship using three archery targets and three practice dummies. On the northwest side of the grounds there are two entrances to the castle's interior, one at ground level guarded by two [Solitude guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard") and one at the top of the wall. The [Thalmor Headquarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Headquarters "Skyrim:Thalmor Headquarters") are located at the top of a large stone staircase on the north side. On the east side of the grounds the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") can be found at ground level. The south side of the castle features the [Emperor's Tower](#Castle_Dour.2C_Emperor.27s_Tower), located between the two main gates. To the right of this is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") with a wooden table beside it with four [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") and two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on top. One of the southeastern sections has a lower secluded area with [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"), a bird's nest containing a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), and a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing") straight across.

### General Tullius's War Room

Antechamber

Entering via the ground floor entrance brings you into an antechamber containing sitting area on the left with a wooden bench against the south wall with a low table in front with a copy of *[Dwemer History and Culture](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_History_and_Culture "Skyrim:Dwemer History and Culture")* on top. Against the east wall is a narrow table with a plate of [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a bowl of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") on top. To your right when entering is a long wooden table with a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* on top and two bookcases beside it holding a couple more common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"). Opposite the entrance are double doors leading into the main command center where [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius"), [Legate Adventus Caesennius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Adventus_Caesennius "Skyrim:Legate Adventus Caesennius") and [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") can normally be found planning the civil war against the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") at all hours. To the right of the doors is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), while to the left is a table with a built-in [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). There are stairs to the north and south.

War Room

The room containing the general and legates has a pair of long wooden tables placed end-to-end with a large tactical map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") showing the progress of the civil war, if any, a copy of *[Mixed Unit Tactics](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixed_Unit_Tactics "Skyrim:Mixed Unit Tactics")* and a couple of [rolls of paper](/wiki/Skyrim:Roll_of_Paper "Skyrim:Roll of Paper"). There are many banners unique to the castle hanging from the walls, while against the east wall, to the left when entering is a narrow table with a bottle of [spiced wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine") on top. To the right is a small cupboard with a bowl of bread and a piece of cheese on top. There are stairs leading up in the middle of the south wall. In the southwest corner are a couple of wooden benches with a low table in front. Against the west wall is a small cupboard with an apprentice-locked display cabinet on top containing an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). In the middle of the north wall is a door leading to the legate's quarters. To the left is a chair and at the rear of the room, in the northwest corner is a small cupboard with a wardrobe and set of shelves in an alcove to the left. On the shelves are two [quicksilver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ingot "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ingot").

Quarters

[Legate Adventus Caesennius'](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Adventus_Caesennius "Skyrim:Legate Adventus Caesennius") quarters consist of one large room separated into three sections. On the right upon entering is a storage area with stacks of cf crates and a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). The middle area is a work area with a wooden table and chair being used as a desk with a copy of *[The City of Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_City_of_Stone "Skyrim:The City of Stone")* on top and two more chairs on the other side. In the northeast corner is a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") with a couple of shelves above holding a bottle of spiced wine and a set of shelves to the left holding a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a common book, a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") and two [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers. To the right of the desk are three bookcases coming out from the north wall partitioning this area from the sleeping area. On the shelves are seven common books and two pieces of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"). Beside these is a corner unit with a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") and a common book on top. To the left beyond the bookcases is the sleeping area containing a single owned bed in the northwest corner, with an end table beside it with a common book on top. A wash basin behind the bookcases and a small wardrobe with two [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and one red apple on top.

General's bedroom

At the top of the stairs to the south is a T-junction with the general's bedroom to the right and a corridor leading to a door outside to the left. The bedroom contains a large owned double bed coming out from the northwestern corner with an end table behind holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and a common book. There are wall shelves above this, one of which holds a bottle of spiced wine, while the other holds an [Imperial helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Helmet"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") and [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Bracers"). At the foot of the bed is a long unlocked non-respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing random items, with a pair of [Imperial boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Boots") beside the bed. Against the west wall is a small wardrobe with two red and a green apple on top. A chair and wooden bench are against the south wall and a narrow table with a wall shelves above holding a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and a wash basin beside it. In the northeastern corner is an alcove with two tall and one small wardrobes all containing fine clothes.

The corridor to the left has a set of shelves against the north wall part way along holding a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), an [Imperial shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Shield"), a pair of Imperial boots and a pair of [Imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots"). The door leads out onto the walls surround [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and the castle courtyard.

### Garrison Barracks

Barracks

The stairs descending to the north from the antechamber leads to the kitchen and barracks for the cities guards and where you will find [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") at night. The kitchen contains three long wooden tables, stacks of crates against the south wall with one of the tables and bench in front. On the table are two pieces of [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef"), three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs, a couple of loaves of bread, a wedge of cheese and an [empty wine bottle](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). In the southeastern corner is a stack of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, with a rack holding two haunches of raw [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat") and one haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") in front. In the middle of the east wall is an oven with an empty metal pot inside. A table is in front with a bucket of [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") underneath. On the table are three [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks, a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two potatoes, a garlic bulb, three loaves of bread and a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"). To the left of the oven are two wall shelves holding three loaves of bread, two potatoes and a sliced eidar cheese, with two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a garlic braid and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging above them. To the left is another stack of food barrels. In front of these is the third table and three chairs, with three pieces of cooked beef, two pieces of bread and three empty wine bottles on top the table.

Storeroom

Opposite the stairs is an unlocked metal gate with a storeroom behind containing sixteen weapon racks on the walls holding many Imperial sword, and at the end is a small unit holding an Imperial helmet, an [Imperial light helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Light Helmet"), an [Imperial cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"), a pairs of [Imperial bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Bracers"), three potions of minor healing, a potion of minor magicka, and a potion of minor stamina. Beside the unit is a pair of Imperial boots on one side and a pair of Imperial light boots and an Imperial shield on the other. A second Imperial shield is against the left-hand wall. To the left at the bottom of the stairs are the sleeping quarters with a round wooden table with a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Rear Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rear_Guard "Skyrim:The Rear Guard")* on top. There are a total of nine single owned beds all coming out from the north and south walls with five end tables between them, mostly empty, but one has a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on top. There are two pairs of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") and two pairs of Imperial boots beside some of the beds and three Imperial helmets and a bottle of wine on shelves above some of the beds.

The stairs descending to the south lead down to a door to *[Castle Dour Dungeon](#Castle_Dour_Dungeon)*.

### Castle Dour Dungeon

Cells

The dungeon is located in the basement of Castle Dour and is circular, and serves as Solitude's [jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Jail "Skyrim:Jail"), where you will be sent if you choose to be jailed to pay for any [crimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") committed in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").

Entering the jail from the Castle above, brings you to a passage that leads onto a balcony above the lowest level where the cell are located. There is a small set of shelves on your left holding some ruined books and a common book. There are several [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing from the walls and ceiling in the dungeon. The balcony circles the rooms below. There are wide pillars at regular intervals around the balcony with a passage either in front or behind. There are many food sacks and barrels against the rear walls with a large coin purse on top of one at the start with a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") on the left. To the north is an unlocked door leading into a guards' rest area, with a small coin purse on a shelving unit and various low-value items scattered about. Beyond this are some chairs and an oven in the outer wall. Beyond this is an end table with a common book on top. To the west is a door leading to a torture chamber. Beyond this is a dresser against the outer wall containing clothes with a [banded iron cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Banded Iron Armor") on top. Next to this are three wall shelves holding a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), some ruined books and four common books. To the south is another door leading to another room. Past this door is a passage leading to stairs descending to the lower level with many barrels, sacks and crates against the walls.

At the bottom of the stairs are some wall shelves opposite holding clutter. The passage continues to the west with a square table on the left holding a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and beyond that is a set of shelves against the northeast wall holding two common books and a leveled potion of healing. The passage turns to the west here and farther along, against the north wall is a set of shelves holding a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), an [iron cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor") and a bottle of wine with a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") beside it. The passage leads around to the passage in front of the cells which are all level-locked, except the one you will be sent to if you are imprisoned, which will always be adept-locked. It contains a hay pile, a bucket containing a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") in the northwestern corner, a square wooden table and two chairs in the northeastern corner and by the southeast corner there is some crumbling mortar that can be activated to escape. Note that activating the crumbling wall will alert nearby [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard"), and cause the nearest one to investigate your cell, so make your way out quickly. The guard will leave the door of your cell open after investigating. This can be useful for a stealth-oriented player, as you can then leave your cell and [pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") the [Castle Dour dungeon key](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon_Key "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon Key") from one of the guards. Thus armed, you can unlock both the personal belongings and evidence chests. The cell to the left of yours is occupied, but you cannot interact with the gate. There are a total of five level-locked cells to the right of your cell.

Following the passage once you have activated the crumbling wall leads past a broken table with rubble crushing it from above with a random potion of stamina on top. Just after this is a chair with a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") on top. The passage descends a long flight of stairs with a barrel partway down with a medium coin purse on top. At the bottom is a small room with a ladder leading back out into Solitude. You come out behind [Angeline's Aromatics](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline%27s_Aromatics "Skyrim:Angeline's Aromatics"), on a level above ground.

The room to the south contains a long wooden table and chair, a set of shelves against the west wall holding two common books, some bread, and cheese, a bunch of lavender and a sprig of snowberries. There is a fireplace in the north wall with some leveled boots nearby, and stair at the back of the room, descending to the south. At the bottom is a round wooden table and two chairs with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top of the table. Against the north wall are several crates and food sacks, while against the west wall are some wall shelves holding an iron sword and [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a pair of [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"), two poisons, and an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"). To the left is a wooden table with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), leveled bracers, a leveled sword, a leveled battleaxe, and a leveled cuirass on top, and a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") underneath. Against the south wall is the evidence chest as well as a leveled warhammer and soul gem, while to the left, in the southeastern corner is a stack of barrels, one of which containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). Against the east wall is a table with the prisoner belongings chest, a soul gem, a weapon, and a shield on top. This table is in front of a hole in the wall, through which you can access the chest if escaping your cell through the crumbling wall.

Torture chamber

The torture chamber to the west contains two small cages hanging from the ceiling, a dead prisoner who can be looted for a few [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") in one of them and a rack between them. Against the north wall is a set of shelves holding some ruined books and a leveled helmet, while at the rear of the room is a table covered in blood, with a leveled dagger on it. The room to the north contains a long wooden table and two chairs with a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a piece of [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat") and a bottle of alto wine on top. At the rear of the room are two sets of shelves holding a total of three common books, an iron cuirass, a pair of [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), an iron helmet, two [iron daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a small coin purse, and a pair of leveled bracers.

### Castle Dour, Emperor's Tower

The entrance to this is separate from the rest of the castle and leads into an audience chamber with a cupboard on your left, a small sitting area on the right consisting of a wooden bench with a low table in front and a small cupboard to the right with a plate of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese and a common [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") on top. A pair of wooden benches and a pair of narrow tables are against the side walls, while at the far end on a raised dais is a large throne. To the right of this is a long unlocked non-respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing random items. Along the east side of the room is a passage leading back to the kitchens, on your left just before the kitchen is a storage area containing barrels, sacks, crates and a set of shelves with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [spiced wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine"), and two bottles of [Honningbrew Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"). The kitchen contains a central [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") with small units on either side and an oven behind. If you are here as part of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire") Then [Gianna](/wiki/Skyrim:Gianna "Skyrim:Gianna") will be standing by the cooking pot, but she won't speak with you until you are wearing a [chef's hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat"). Against the east wall are some shelves that hold several chef's hats and have two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids hanging in front. To the right are more shelves holding several loaves of bread and a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), with two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a garlic braid and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging in front. To the south are more shelves holding a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a potato, many pieces of cheese, several loaves of bread, a fillet of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, and a [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"). Hanging above these shelves are six bunches of dried elves ear, a garlic braid and a bunch of frost mirriam.

When standing behind the cooking pot facing north, on the right-hand unit is two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), two [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), six [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), three bulbs of garlic, two [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), a fillet of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"), a bottle of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")*. While hanging over it are two bunches of dried elves ear, two garlic braids and a bunch of dried frost mirriam. At the end are three open crates in a stack containing three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of wine and two [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). On the left-hand unit are two [giant's toes](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a bulb of garlic, a bowl of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") and two [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). Hanging over this are three whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and an open crate beside it containing four potatoes. Against the west wall are two more open crates stacked on top of each other, the top one holds two wheels of cheese, and the bottom one contains a gourd, a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus, an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). South of these are more shelves holding a fillet of horker meat, a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), a rack of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), two [charred skeever hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), and several pieces of cheese. Hanging in front of these is a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a salmon, two haunches of raw [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat") and a haunch of raw venison. To the west are two more open crates containing loaves of bread and wheels of cheese. South of these are more [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels.

Against the west wall of the audience chamber is a narrow wooden table with a stone bowl containing a bunch of lavender, a bulb of garlic, a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") on top. To the left are stairs leading up to a passage with a door ahead and the passage turning to the left. The passage overlooks the room below. At the far end is a room that is locked and requires a key.--This is a dining room and can only be accessed during the related quest. In front of this is a sitting area with two wooden benches with a low table in front and a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")*. The room at the other end of the passage is the Emperor's sleeping quarters and contains a large owned four-poster double bed coming out from the southwest corner, with a long unlocked non-respawning chest containing random items at the foot of the bed and an end table to the right with a common book on top. Against the west wall is a small wardrobe with a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), and a [green](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and two red apples on top. There is a chair against the north wall and a wooden bench and wash basin against the west wall. Against the south wall is another bench, a narrow table to the left and beside this a corner unit with a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") on top. Opposite this is a dressing area containing two tall wardrobes containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes").

## Notes

- Infinite [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") can be obtained by watching the guards practice archery. Just take the arrows from the targets they use for practice.
- If the guards see you practicing along with them, they may say things like "Hey, watch it!", "Be careful!", and "Don't do that."
  - Even then, you won't get a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") unless you hit one of them in the process.
- There is an  "Escape") Escape [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") in the dungeon on the floor next to the collapsible wall. The escape route is behind that collapsible wall.
- If [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") is completed, [Istar Cairn-Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Istar_Cairn-Breaker "Skyrim:Istar Cairn-Breaker") will move to Castle Dour.
- Should the Stormcloaks win the Civil War, guard patrols inside Castle Dour will be comparatively lax - the Imperial guards that used to patrol the interior and guard the door will not be replaced. The same is true for the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") should the Empire win the war - the guards patrolling the upstairs living quarters will not be replaced after the Empire wins the war.
- There was initially going to be an extra area in Castle Dour, called [Castle Dour, Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#Castle_Dour.2C_Tower "Skyrim:Test Cells"), which would have connected the main area of the castle (with the entrance being in General Tullius' bedroom) to the top of the tower which is currently inaccessible. Game data indicates that this area would have been used as an escape route by General Tullius in the Battle of Solitude, leading to a final showdown with him on the battlements. This area still exists and is completely furnished, but inaccessible.
- All end tables, cupboards, and dressers in the location are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- The two Imperial guards who stand watch outside are called "Solitude Guards", even though they don't wear the city guard armor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. They are now called "Imperial Guards".
- One of the doors to the Emperor's Tower is not properly locked prior to [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire") which can cause some of the quest triggers inside to break.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- Some of items in the Dungeon are marked as owned by the MarkarthHagsCureFaction, making them free to take if you help [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela"). **?**
- Two of the wardrobes in the upstairs of the Emperor's tower are set inside other containers; another wardrobe and a cupboard, respectively. In order to access the other container, the crosshairs have to be oriented just right so that the "open" option appears. **?**
- After completing Battle for Solitude, the Imperial banners don't change for the Stormcloak ones. **?**

# Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns

## Overview

Castle Karstaag Caverns

**Castle Karstaag Caverns** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") on the north coast of Solstheim containing [bristlebacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback") and [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"). It contains only one zone, *[Castle Karstaag Caverns](#Castle_Karstaag_Caverns).*

## Related Quests

- **[Paid in Full](/wiki/Skyrim:Paid_in_Full "Skyrim:Paid in Full")**: Recover the [bonemold formula](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Formula "Skyrim:Bonemold Formula") for [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory").

### Exterior

The entrance is southeast of [Castle Karstaag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins") above a tall waterfall that plunges to an inlet by the sea. The path to the entrance descends from the west-southwest to the stream feeding the waterfall, with a second stream flowing from the entrance joining the first at the top of the waterfall.

### Castle Karstaag Caverns

Entrance tunnel

The entrance leads into a tunnel with a stream flowing down the right side and a path to the left. A [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush is just inside the entrance. The path leads west past a pair of ice pillars to a short waterfall dropping from above, with an opening to the south connecting to a huge cavern. The cavern features three bridges at different heights over a lake; several rieklings can be seen running across the bridges. To the left on a patch of ice in the lake is the corpse of [Esmond Tyne](/wiki/Skyrim:Esmond_Tyne "Skyrim:Esmond Tyne"), the target for [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory")'s [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Paid_in_Full "Skyrim:Paid in Full").

Main cavern

If you dive into the water and swim due south, you will eventually find an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a leveled [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"). A method of [waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(effect) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (effect)") and a [light](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight") spell are recommended. Opposite the body of Esmond Tyne, an ice ramp ascends from the water to the west side of the lowest bridge. Across the bridge to the east is the first of several riekling camps. One riekling patrols the bridge, a second wanders the camp, and a third stands on a lookout platform at the back of the camp.

In the camp on the east side of the bridge, a tent on the right contains a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and (like most riekling tents) a hay pile that can be used to sleep. The lookout platform contains two coin purses, one medium and one small. Just north of the platform is a [riekling hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Hut "Skyrim:Riekling Hut"), another tent, and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") next to an ingredient barrel.

Returning to the west side of the bridge, the ice ramp connects to a narrow tunnel ascending to the west, with two rieklings on a ledge above to the right. The tunnel soon turns north and emerges in a small chamber. To the right, a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") lies among the rocks in a dead end. To the left, three rieklings stand near a campfire below a fenced ledge. To the west is a short tunnel leading to a door.

Beyond the door, the tunnel becomes partly flooded and turns north. Just past the turn, a novice-locked door to the right opens to a cell containing a large coin purse and a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). The tunnel continues to a fork. To the right heading east is another door, while to the left heading west are two more doors to the north and south. The novice-locked north door reveals a cell containing an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). The apprentice-locked south door opens to another cell containing a dead riekling, a bundle of riekling spears, and a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick").

Beyond the door to the east, another tunnel ascends, turns south, and emerges on the ledge above the previous campfire. To the right are three barrels, with a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), a random [healing potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a random potion among the barrels. To the left, the ledge continues into a short tunnel leading east to a riekling camp on another ledge above the lake. As you exit the tunnel, a riekling will burst from the snow ahead, and a second will emerge from a tent behind the first. To the right of the tunnel exit are two crates, one of which has a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") on top, with a quiver of random [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") and a sack among the crates. To the left of the tunnel exit is a food barrel, another barrel, a sack, and another tent. Northeast of the tent is a lookout platform containing a riekling and a medium coin purse. Near the first tent from which the riekling had emerged is a third tent and a bridge crossing the cavern to the east. Beyond the bridge on the near side, the narrow ledge to the south turns west around a corner to a ledge above the two rieklings near the west side of the first bridge. This higher ledge features a riekling hut and three random soul gems, two of which are filled, on the ground or in a toppled basin.

Bristleback cavern

To the east on the far side of the bridge are three tents, with rieklings in two of the tents. Next to the first tent at the end of the bridge is a food barrel, another barrel, and a sack. Just to the north, the second tent contains a random war axe. To the south is the third tent and a riekling hut. To the east, a tunnel ascends to a fenced ledge overlooking another cavern. Along the fence are three collections of barrels, crates, and sacks, which include two food barrels, three sacks, and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") and a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") on one of the crates. To the south, the ledge connects to another tunnel leading back to the west. To the north, the ledge descends to the main level of the cavern, which contains a lookout platform, a riekling, an open pen holding three [bristlebacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback"), and a waterfall near the southeast wall. Outside the pen are two food barrels, three sacks, and a crate, with a random potion next to the crate, while an alcove to the southwest contains a novice-locked chest and a large coin purse.

The tunnel leading west at the top of the ledge ends at a door that opens onto another ledge above the lake. The ledge features a riekling in a tent, a [riekling barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Barrel "Skyrim:Riekling Barrel") next to two crates, and a bridge crossing the cavern to the west. On the far side of the bridge is a small ledge, where a second bridge crosses to the southwest to a pair of tents and a riekling hut guarded by two more rieklings. The tent nearest the hut contains a random [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), with a chest next to the tent. Near the tent and chest is a small stream fed by three waterfalls at the top of a large waterfall plunging to the lake below. Across the stream is a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), a leveled mace, and a leveled [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). Another lootable skeleton hangs over the edge of the ledge above the stream between two of the three waterfalls; the skeleton can be dislodged using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). A chest, a large coin purse, and a random sword on the same ledge can be reached by careful use of the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout. Another coin purse can be found on a ledge under the bridge.

North of the two tents near the end of the second bridge, climbing the ice leads to another ledge. Beyond a narrow gap to the northeast is a piece of random [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), a medium coin purse, and an adept-locked chest. Returning to the two tents, a door to the west leads to a tunnel which ascends and turns north. Just past the turn is a small fence surrounding a sack, two unusable barrels, and two crates, with a leveled [potion of resist cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Cold "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Cold"), a leveled healing potion, a pair of leveled [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), a small coin purse, and the [Castle Kaarstag key](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Key "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Key") among the barrels and crates. At the top of the tunnel is the exit to [Castle Karstaag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins").

## Notes

- The three random soul gems on the ledge may have fallen into the snow and not be visible, but searching the snow will enable you to retrieve them.
- The chest on the ledge at the top of the cavern can be reached by climbing on top of the hut next to the stream, using Whirlwind Sprint into the nearby wall to the southeast, and using [mountain climbing](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") techniques to ascend the rest of the way.
- The Castle Kaarstag key opens the master-locked exit to Solstheim from Castle Karstaag Ruins.
- Castle Karstaag Caverns also appears in the [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon") expansion for *[Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind")*, as part of the interior of [Castle Karstaag](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Castle_Karstaag "Bloodmoon:Castle Karstaag").

## Bugs

- You may become stuck in an icy crevice in the bristleback cavern. The crevice is above the bristleback pen, on the far side of the fence near the crate holding the apothecary's satchel and random helmet.

## Gallery

# Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins

## Overview

Castle Karstaag Ruins

**Castle Karstaag Ruins** is an icy clearing outside [Castle Karstaag Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Caverns "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns").

It was once a large frozen keep, but time has ravaged the structure since the slaying of its master, the frost giant [Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag "Skyrim:Karstaag"). It is now overrun by [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling").

## Related Quests

- **[Summoning Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoning_Karstaag "Skyrim:Summoning Karstaag")**: Summon and defeat [Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag "Skyrim:Karstaag").

## Castle Karstaag Ruins

Rieklings

The usual path to the ruins is through Castle Karstaag Caverns. Upon exiting the cavern, a leveled [mounted riekling](/wiki/Skyrim:Mounted_Riekling "Skyrim:Mounted Riekling") is in front of you, and to your left on the north side of the clearing are two more rieklings near the throne holding the skeleton of Karstaag. To the south is a master-locked door leading to the rest of the island, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Key "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Key") to which is carried by the mounted riekling. If you have already found [Karstaag's skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Karstaag's Skull"), you can activate the throne, which will return the skull to the skeleton and summon Karstaag to rise as a ghostly frost giant.

## Notes

- Castle Karstaag is the name given to a [map icon](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Castle_Karstaag.png "File:SR-mapicon-Castle Karstaag.png") in the game files added by [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), but the map icon was not used in the game.
- Castle Karstaag also appears in [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Castle_Karstaag "Bloodmoon:Castle Karstaag"), as an intact structure.

# Skyrim:Castle Volkihar

## Overview

This article is about the dungeon portions of Castle Volkihar which contain enemies. For the portion of the castle inhabited by the Volkihar vampire clan, see [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep").
