Castle Volkihar

**Castle Volkihar** is a large [castle](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") on an island far northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") connected to [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"). The dungeon areas of the castle, most of which contain enemies, include four interior zones: *[Volkihar Undercroft](#Volkihar_Undercroft)*, *[Volkihar East Tower](#Volkihar_East_Tower)*, *[Volkihar North Tower](#Volkihar_North_Tower)*, and *[Volkihar Ruins](#Volkihar_Ruins)* including *[Valerica's Study](#Valerica.27s_Study)*, and two additional external zones: *[Volkihar Courtyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Courtyard "Skyrim:Volkihar Courtyard")* and *Castle Volkihar Balcony*. Castle Volkihar Balcony is displayed on the map as a  [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+Balcony&zoom=14&legacy=true), which is the nearest fast-travel point to Valerica's study and the portal to the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn"). Castle Volkihar and Castle Volkihar Balcony count as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic.

Though you can travel to the island immediately upon installing [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), the dungeon areas of the castle are initially inaccessible due to the external door being locked and requiring a key. To reach the island, either hire the rowboat at [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") or use the one at [Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty"). Your other options are to swim or walk on the surface of the water using either a [Potion of Waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Potion of Waterwalking") or [Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Boots_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking"). If you accept Lord Harkon's gift at the end of [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline"), you can also float over to the island in [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") form. If you swim, walk, or float to the island from Icewater Jetty, you may encounter two groups of three or four hostile [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") on the way. These skeletons will rise out of the water and attack when they detect you.

The travel spawn point for Castle Volkihar is at the southwest end of the island, near a tower and the pier that returns you to Icewater Jetty. To reach the castle's entrance, walk northeast from the island pier. There will be a gate blocking your way which will not be opened until near the end of Bloodline. Once you have entered the castle during Bloodline and chosen whether to accept or reject Lord Harkon's gift, the castle will either be open or locked to you, respectively. If you rejected Lord Harkon's gift, you will be teleported out of the castle, and the door will remain locked until the start of the quest [Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes").

## Related Quests

- **[Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline")**: Choose your side!
- **[Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes")**: Explore Castle Volkihar.

### Exterior

Exterior

If you accept Lord Harkon's gift, whenever you arrive at the castle on subsequent visits, you may find two or more hostile Dawnguard waiting near the travel spawn point at the southwest end of the island. If you have remained undetected, one of these Dawnguard may be patrolling the northwest shore of the island, while the other can usually be found on top of the tower.

With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found at the pier, along with a bucket of [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull") and a fishing rod. Fish that can be found in freezing waters can be found here. Follow the shoreline to the left of the castle until you reach a crumbling, disused dock, where there are several sunken boats and ships. The docks are guarded by four leveled [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") armed with [ancient Nord weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Draugr_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"), which may be honed. They are significantly tougher than typical skeletons; most are magic-users, and graphically they appear to be wearing armor. There are plenty of [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") that can be fished from the docks. Deep below the water is an overturned sunken ship with a broken keel. The hull has split open just enough to grant access below deck. Among some crates is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. Unless you are an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian"), in order to reach the chest you will need to use a [waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(effect) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (effect)") effect via a [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Potion of Waterbreathing") or enchantment. A [light](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight") spell would also be a boon. To locate the ship, swim from the far end of the docks to the northwest. With Fishing, some [vampire fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Fish "Skyrim:Vampire Fish") can be found swimming off the docks here. There are numerous stairs rising up from the docks to terraces far above. At the top is an entrance to *[Volkihar Undercroft](#Volkihar_Undercroft)*, which is locked prior to starting the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes").

### Volkihar Undercroft

The water cistern found shortly after entering the undercroft

The entrance leads to a balcony, with stairs descending on the left. There is a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") wandering this area, which will attack as soon as it is aware of you. You'll also find seven loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and some [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat") on the floor among the straw and bones. The stairs descend to a landing, with a barrel of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") stuck into the top by a stone railing. On the right are some crates and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks beside the wall. There is an unlocked wooden door in front of you to the north, with stairs leading down on the left to large double doors also to the north. The single door opens onto a balcony overlooking the old water cistern, which can be used to snipe those in the next room. The double doors lead into the same room at floor level. There are up to five [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound") and a [feral vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Feral_Vampire "Skyrim:Feral Vampire") inhabiting this area. The feral vampire is carrying a [journal fragment](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_Fragment "Skyrim:Journal Fragment"), which explains how she's been taking control of the keep's death hounds and promises revenge against the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") living in the keep. If you return here after the quest, only the death hounds respawn.

The central third of the room is sunken, and was originally used to collect water for the cistern. There are stairs descending down into it at the far end. On either side are paths, with a stone bridge linking them near the balcony. There are alcoves on either side, with grating over water-filled tunnels. Just beyond the first alcove on the left is a barrel of ingredients. In the southeastern corner are four coffins and a dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers"). You can loot the two closed coffins, the draugr, and a skeleton in one of the two open coffins. There is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") in the bottom of the other open coffin (see [bugs](#Bugs)). The first alcove on the right contains an adept-[trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") chest, which triggers [spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") to thrust up from the grating in the floor. To avoid damage, either [disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") it before opening the chest, or simply stand at the bottom of the stairs and not in the alcove. At the back of the room, stairs ascend to a higher level that continues around to the west. An [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") is to the left of stairs up into another room, with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") and a bottle of [weak aversion to magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Magic "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Magic") [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") on top. To the right of the stairs is a set of shelves holding a pair of [vampire gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Vampire Gauntlets"), a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet"), [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a salt pile, and a food sack. The room up the stairs has a small table and chair on the right, and a barrel of ingredients in the back right corner beside a narrow table against the rear wall. On the table is a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")*, a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*, a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and a rarely seen item of clutter, a [bloody tankard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloody_Tankard "Skyrim:Bloody Tankard"). Under the table is a pair of [vampire boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Boots "Skyrim:Vampire Boots"). To the left of the table is an upright coffin you can sleep if you are a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism"). To the left of the coffin is a small shelving unit that holds a small coin purse and a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"). On the left is a lever on a small balcony, with a path below heading west from the main room. There is a raised bridge blocking this lower path, which is operated by the lever.

Below are stakes ready to impale intruders

The path heading west has an alcove on the left containing an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") near a skeletal hand protruding from under grating in the wall. Once the bridge is lowered, the path continues to the middle of the next room, which features fire-hardened [stakes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Pit "Skyrim:Spike Pit") in a partially flooded area around you. If you fall down, there is a passage leading back up in the northwest corner of the room. Take care however to avoid the stakes, as they can inflict a significant amount of damage. The passage has four bear traps along its length, and a skeever wandering the passage unless it has fallen afoul of one of the traps. Near the top of the passage is a skeletal magic-user armed with an ancient Nord weapon. There is another raised bridge in front of you to the west, and a path heading south past three strings of [infected bones](/wiki/Skyrim:Infected_Bones "Skyrim:Infected Bones"). If you are neither vampire nor [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf"), take special care, as you will risk a significant chance of contracting at least one [disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Diseases "Skyrim:Diseases") by touching the bones. Once past the infected bones, the passage turns to the west, passing an easily avoided string of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") and leading into a split-leveled room with piles of bones covering most of the floor and bookcases filled with [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") flanking the doorway. Up to three death hounds inhabit this room, which has balconies on most sides. There are stairs rising to the south. As you enter the room, a trap door opens in the ceiling to allow more gory bones to fall to join the piles below.

Nope

The stairs lead up to a landing serving as a torture area, with shackles bolted to the wall, and blood splattered on the wall and floor below. Two small wardrobes contain a selection of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), on top of which is a bottle of [weak lingering poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Lingering_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Lingering Poison"), a phial of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a [potion of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), two salt piles, some leather strips, and a woodcutter's axe. More stairs lead up to a passage heading east, which then turns north. At this point, you are faced with two thick walls of cobwebs that you need to hack or burn your way through to the north and east. The eastern webs conceal an adept-locked chest, while the northern webs block the passage where a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider") lurks in a room containing a barrel of ingredients and the second lever needed to lower the previous raised bridge. A grating behind the lever looks down on the bridges. Before returning and taking this new path, there is a wooden door to the west that opens onto one of the balconies in the previous room. Opposite is another balcony that can be reached if you are a [vampire lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") using your Bats lesser power, or with at least two words of the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). You can also reach it by jumping from the bone pile in the northwest corner of the room. This balcony features a skeleton with a random potion of healing in its hand, with a medium coin purse and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") beside it. At the other end of the balcony is an unlocked chest. Once you've looted these items, you can drop to the bone-filled room below and return to the partially flooded room to cross the recently lowered bridge. From here, make your way up several flights of stairs to a door leading outside to *[Volkihar Courtyard](#Volkihar_Courtyard)*.

### Volkihar Courtyard

Through the door are steps leading up into the courtyard, which has obviously been left untouched for countless years, as it was once the domain of Serana's mother [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica"). [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") will inform you that something is wrong with the large moondial on the ground, which is many paces wide and in the center of the courtyard. It appears three of the crests are missing, namely, the [Full Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Full_Moon_Crest "Skyrim:Full Moon Crest"), [Half Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Half_Moon_Crest "Skyrim:Half Moon Crest"), and [Crescent Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescent_Moon_Crest "Skyrim:Crescent Moon Crest") crests. Serana will inform you if questioned that the moondial was crafted for her mother by an elven artisan from an old sundial that was placed here by the previous occupants of the castle, and that it was special to her mother. There are many dead trees and gravestones around the edges of the courtyard, with stairs leading up to doors to the southeast, northeast, and west. The door to the west has collapsed due to a cave-in, allowing no access through there. In fact, the courtyard has suffered quite a bit of damage, which Serana will suggest was caused by her [father](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon"), who likely went on a rampage when she and her mother left, blocking off anything which reminded him of his wife and daughter.

View of the courtyard with completed moondial

There are gargoyle statues near each of the exits from the courtyard, either above the doors or on the railings of the stairs leading to them, but none burst to life. There are many [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing from the limbs of the trees and down the walls that surround the courtyard. To the northwest is a small pool of water, with five tufts of [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass"), four [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), and one patch of [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") fungus growing around the edge. In the middle of the pool is a large rock, with the missing half moon crest lying on it. There is a planter containing a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") plant and another with [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") at the top of stairs to the northeast, on either side of the door to *[Volkihar North Tower](#Volkihar_North_Tower)*. To the right of the door are stairs leading up to a terrace with a large planter on your right containing a patch each of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") and blisterwort fungi. A wooden bench is to the left, and against the railing past the planter is a large round table and chairs, which would once have been a pleasant place to sit. Beside the table, the missing crescent moon crest lies on the ground. At the rear of this terrace is another cave-in, with piles of masonry and rubble. To the south is another planter, this one empty. Beside the planter are more stairs leading down to the door to *[Volkihar East Tower](#Volkihar_East_Tower)*. The stairs across the courtyard to the west lead up to more terraces, with planters containing a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") and another patch of blisterwort fungus at either end, as well as more tables and chairs. To the east are nine [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants growing in a small walled garden, with the missing full moon crest among the vegetation.

During the related quest, Serana will stand by the moondial, allowing you to explore both of the towers unaccompanied. For more details on the courtyard, see [Volkihar Courtyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Courtyard "Skyrim:Volkihar Courtyard").

### Volkihar East Tower

Entering the east tower

You access this tower from *Volkihar Courtyard*, through the door to the east. It consists of only one room filled with rubble and crushed skeletons which cannot be looted. There are no enemies in this tower, only several flights of stairs leading up to the rear. At the very top of the stairs, partially buried by masonry that has crushed a skeleton, is a medium coin purse, an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), a [sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(item) "Skyrim:Sapphire (item)"), and eleven loose septims littering the steps. Down one flight of stairs and behind the rubble to the west is an unlocked wooden chest containing minor loot. There is nothing else of value in this tower.

### Volkihar North Tower

The north tower hosts a large room

This is the larger of the two towers accessible from the courtyard, through the door to the north. Through the door is a room containing empty furniture and stairs descending to the east. In front of you is a doorway out onto a balcony above a large room containing two skeletons. One is standing at the bottom of the stairs opposite, facing the balcony you're on, while the other is sitting on a bench in front of the fireplace below you to the left, facing away from you. The balcony is an ideal sniping point to deal with both of these foes. The stairs to the east lead down to a smaller room containing another skeleton sitting on a bench, with two small wardrobes containing a selection of fine clothes on either side of an adept-locked door. There is also a doorway to the west leading to the lower level of the room beneath the balcony.

Behind the locked door is a flight of stairs blocked by a cave-in, with a crushed skeleton beneath the masonry holding a [silver jeweled necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Jeweled_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Jeweled Necklace"), and two [gold ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot") and a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet") on the stairs beside it. Through the doorway into the larger room, [gargoyle](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle") statues sit in the northeast and northwest corners of the room. However, only the one in the northeast corner will burst to life and attack you when it detects your presence. To the left of this gargoyle is an unlocked wooden chest. Farther to the left, up the steps to the far north through the open double doors, more fallen masonry blocks more stairs, with an expert-locked chest among the rubble. Along the west wall to the right of the fireplace is a set of shelves, with a [flawless garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Garnet "Skyrim:Flawless Garnet") hidden among clutter on one of the shelves. Under a balcony in the southwest corner is a wall shelf holding a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"). This second balcony can be reached using either Whirlwind Sprint or the vampire lord Bats power, and features an unlocked chest among more fallen masonry.

### Volkihar Ruins

An apparent dead end with a hidden door

This zone cannot be accessed until you complete the moondial puzzle in the courtyard during the related quest. Upon replacing the three crests, a spiraling stairwell descends around the center of the dial to reveal a door, in similar fashion to the passages to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") found using the [attunement sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") on the Dwarven mechanisms at the end of [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"), [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"), and [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar"). Through the door at the bottom is a passage, with stairs leading up to a dead end. There are shelving units on either side holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and two coin purses, one small and one medium. There is also a pull chain to the left, which opens a concealed door in front of you. (Note that if you are returning to the dungeon after having completed the associated quest, do NOT pull the chain again, as this will close the secret door, but not reopen it (see [bugs](#Bugs)).) There are three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") on the floor behind the concealed door. The room beyond is used as some type of kitchen, with a bloody table in the middle covered with bones and gore. Around the room are several counters, wall shelves, and tables, all covered in gory detritus, as well as a total of six salt piles, a piece of canis root, a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), and a woodcutter's axe. Hanging from the ceiling is a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), and a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"). In the middle of the east wall is an old extinguished fireplace containing three more pieces of firewood, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front which can strangely still be used to [cook](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking"). To the right is an alcove filled with unusable barrels, while to the left is a flight of blood-covered stairs that lead up to a door. During the related quest, Serana will start stating from this point onwards that *"We're getting close, I'm sure of it"*.

A dining room that hosts several skeletons

Through the door is a large dining room containing a long run of tables placed end-to-end; seven skeletons sit at the tables, most of the tougher type that appear to be wearing armor. As soon as you enter the room, the room will light up as if there was a light source over the table, and the twin fires in the fireplaces to the east will also light. There are [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") on the table and scattered on the floor, along with several narrow tables and sets of shelves against the walls. A drum and [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") are by the south wall, on or in front of a set of shelves. There are raised sections with stairs leading up to them at either end of the room. There is nothing of interest on the raised section to the north, only another blocked passage. On the southern section are some wooden benches and a small bookcase filled with ruined books. To the left of the bookcase is a flight of stairs leading up to a heavily vaulted room, with thin cobwebs and strings of infected bones hanging from the ceiling. On the far side of the room is a leveled gargoyle, with braziers on either side. As soon as you enter far enough into the room, these will light up, and the gargoyle will burst to life and attack. The only items of note in the room are a couple of leather strips; one is in the middle of the floor, and the other is on a narrow table to the right of a door in the southwestern corner. In the southeastern corner is another passage, but it is blocked just around the corner by fallen masonry.

The door in the southwest corner opens into another room, with several wall shelves on the wall opposite holding various animal and human skulls all the way up to a shelf high overhead holding the skull of a [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth"). To the right of this wall are wide stairs up to a raised section, where two armored skeletons sit on benches. To the right of the benches is a series of flights of stairs leading up. To the left is an adept-locked wooden door, which opens to a small cupboard containing a barrel of ingredients with some leather strips on top, as well as a set of shelves holding a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), two [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), four loose septims, and a cast iron pot hiding a sapphire, an amethyst, and a small coin purse.

The braziers above light up mysteriously

As soon as you start climbing the long flight of stairs, rows of braziers on either side will light up. Around the corner to the left are two more strings of infected bones hanging from the ceiling, while two nearby desks against the wall hold seven loose septims on a plate, a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina, a sapphire, and a flute. Above the desks is a small balcony, and nearby just out of sight are a couple of armored skeletons. To the right, in the southern corner, is a leveled gargoyle that will burst to life and attack as soon as you are near. The balcony can be reached by following the room to the right of the desks, passing under a fallen piece of masonry, and climbing the stairs beyond. At the top, on the right is an inert statue of a gargoyle, while on the left is an open door. There are more stairs ahead at the back of the room, but they only lead to two empty planters, with a balcony high above patrolled by at least one armored skeleton.

Through the door, on the right is a blocked stairway, while to the left is an open door. Past the open door, two small wardrobes against the left wall contain more fine clothes. Beyond the wardrobes in the southern corner are a small balcony and an adept-locked door. Through the locked door is the previous balcony above the desks, with an unlocked chest in the corner. Looking back at the door through which you originally entered this room, you will see a shield rack mounted above the door holding a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") and crossed [iron greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"). Against the right wall are more stairs leading up to an area with a chair and table holding a [common book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), a piece of [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather"), and some small shelves at the back of the table holding some [rolls of paper](/wiki/Skyrim:Roll_of_Paper "Skyrim:Roll of Paper"), a [scroll of fire storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm"), and two lockpicks. There is another common book on the floor, beside the chair. To the left of the table is a set of shelves holding a further seven common books and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"). To the northwest is an open door into a larger room, with two long unlocked chests against the right wall, two doorways on the left wall, and a third doorway in the back right northern corner. Both of the small rooms on the left are bedrooms, but both beds have been broken and buried by falling masonry and are now unusable. The only item of interest in either room is a wardrobe containing fine clothes in the second room.

Through the door in the northern corner is a flight of stairs leading up to a door. The room beyond is another dining room, with several raised sections. There are three armored skeletons in this room. Behind the door to the left is a small wardrobe containing yet more fine clothes. To the right a set of stairs descends to the main part of the room, where two long wooden tables are arranged with chairs along either side. There is a blocked passage to the southeast, and a wider passage to the northwest that is also blocked. At the rear of the room is a raised section, with stairs along the rear wall leading up to it. At the top, on the left is a lowered wooden portcullis, while at the far end is another leveled gargoyle, with a pull chain behind it. As soon as you pull the chain, the gargoyle will burst to life and attack. There is also an armored skeleton through a door in the southern corner, standing on the small balcony over the two empty planters seen previously. On either side of the gargoyle and in an alcove to the east are several sets of shelves, desks, and a table and chairs, but these only hold clutter.

A chapel lies beyond the portcullis

Once the gargoyle has been dealt with, you can pass under the now raised portcullis. A pull chain on the right operates it from this side. Wide stairs rise to the northwest, with an armored skeleton partway up the stairs, just past a large piece of masonry. There seems to be quite a lot of sunlight coming through windows along the right side of the stairs. As you near the top of the stairs, yet another leveled gargoyle will burst to life and attack. On the left is another lowered wooden portcullis and a chapel beyond, with the chain to operate it on the right. Ahead to the northwest is an expert-locked wooden door. Regardless of which route you take, you will end up in the same place. If you choose to raise the portcullis and enter the chapel, however, you will have to backtrack to complete the exploration, making the route through the expert-locked door preferable if you want to conveniently fully explore this area and collect all the treasure available.

The chapel has a walkway forming an arch overhead, with an armored skeleton patrolling back and forth across it. There are also balconies on both sides of the room with a skeleton on each, and underneath are two more armored skeletons sitting on benches. The chapel is in shambles, with pews piled up in two large heaps. Behind the pulpit is a wooden screen, with an unlocked chest behind it in the eastern corner, and a small cupboard opposite containing a few septims and clutter.

A hidden armory containing an assortment of weapons

Through the expert-locked door is a passage leading up, around a corner, and into an armory. There are a total of twenty-five weapon racks on the walls, which hold fourteen ancient Nord weapons, a random enchanted [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), and a random enchanted [two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [melee weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"). There are four wooden benches down the center of the room backed by screens, and four sets of shelves holding three random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina, a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), two bottles of alto wine, and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). To the southwest is a short flight of stairs up to a third portcullis, again with the chain to the right. Past this is another blocked flight of stairs ahead, with a doorway on the left. Through this door is a passage that links the chapel, balconies, and raised walkway. The balcony on this side is right in front of the doorway, with the other balcony directly opposite, while the walkway can be reached to the left, and the chapel below can be accessed to the right. Any fighting is likely to alert all the skeletons to your presence. Once you've dealt with all foes and explored the chapel below, crossing the walkway leads to a passage and a series of stairs up to an unlocked door.

The room at the top has a row of tables laid end-to-end, with an unlootable skeleton laid out with various other bones and skulls. There is a long unlocked chest against the southwest wall, as well as several small tables and chairs and a few sets of shelves around the room, but the only item of interest is a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina on a shelf against the northwest wall, to the left of yet another door. Through this door is a blocked passageway on the right, and stairs leading up on the left to large double doors.

Gargoyles lie still, ready to ambush

These doors open into a large room with a high vaulted ceiling. Five gargoyle statues are seated in the room: one on the left, two in the middle, and two on the right. One of each of these will burst to life when approached, one of which is the highest level possible. Once they are dealt with, during the quest, Serana will wonder if you are at the top yet, and whether there is a secret entrance in the room. There is a long wooden table in the center of the room, with two iron daggers and an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") on top. In the southern corner are two unowned upright coffins, which you can sleep in if you are a vampire. Between the coffins is a small wardrobe containing fine clothes and featuring a set of shelves on top, with the shelves holding a set of the rare [vampire royal armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Royal_Armor "Skyrim:Vampire Royal Armor") and a [silver sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Sword "Skyrim:Silver Sword"); beside the wardrobe on the floor is a pair of [vampire boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Boots "Skyrim:Vampire Boots"). In a small raised area against the rear wall are two sets of shelves filled with more empty wine bottles, with the shelves on the right also holding a [scroll of conjure familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Familiar"). There are three pieces of firewood laid in what appears to be a fireplace, but if you turn the wall-mounted candlestick on the left, the fireplace wall will open to reveal another passage. Follow a series of flights of stairs as you climb, winding around with each flight, to a door at the top. Through the door is *[Valerica's Study](#Valerica.27s_Study).*

#### Valerica's Study

Valerica's study is a large room on two levels, with a large circular indentation in the floor surrounded by candles in the center of the lower level. This is where the portal to the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") opens during the quest [Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes"). Stairs against the southeast wall lead up to the raised section in the northeast. After the death of [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon"), if you choose to inform Valerica, she will again take up residence here.

Valerica's library

In the western corner is a small library. A row of bookshelves against the rear wall must have been impressive, but time has ruined many of the books, leaving few books intact in addition to *[Valerica's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Valerica's Journal")*:

:   **Books**

:   |  |  |  |  |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | - *[2920, Sun's Dusk, v11](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dusk,_v11 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dusk, v11")* (two copies) - *[Feyfolken I](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_I "Skyrim:Feyfolken I")* - *[Feyfolken II](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_II "Skyrim:Feyfolken II")* - *[Feyfolken III](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_III "Skyrim:Feyfolken III")* | - *[Forge, Hammer and Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge,_Hammer_and_Anvil "Skyrim:Forge, Hammer and Anvil")* - *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")* - *[Opusculus Lamae Bal](/wiki/Skyrim:Opusculus_Lamae_Bal "Skyrim:Opusculus Lamae Bal")* - *[Pirate King of the Abecean](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_King_of_the_Abecean "Skyrim:Pirate King of the Abecean")* | - *[Rising Threat, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. I")* - *[Ruins of Kemel-Ze](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Kemel-Ze "Skyrim:Ruins of Kemel-Ze")* - *[The Dowry](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dowry "Skyrim:The Dowry")* - *[The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v2 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2")* | - *[The True Nature of Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:The_True_Nature_of_Orcs "Skyrim:The True Nature of Orcs")* - *[The Windhelm Letters](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Windhelm_Letters "Skyrim:The Windhelm Letters")* - *[The Wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wispmother "Skyrim:The Wispmother")* - *[Watcher of Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Watcher_of_Stones "Skyrim:Watcher of Stones")* |

Against the southwest wall to the left of the library is a long wooden table with a built-in alchemy lab. Also found on the table among bones and skulls both human and animal, including a [dragon bone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bone "Skyrim:Dragon Bone") (see [notes](#Notes)), are two bowls of normal [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and a stone bowl containing [finely ground bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Finely_Ground_Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Finely Ground Bone Meal"). This last item is not an ingredient, but will be found under the miscellaneous section of your character's inventory menu, and is needed to create a portal to the Soul Cairn. In the southern corner is a short flight of stairs ascending to a door leading outside onto the *Volkihar Balcony*, which is the nearest fast-travel location to the portal leading to the Soul Cairn. The first time you use the door, a map marker is added to your in-game map as a fast-travel point named *Castle Volkihar Balcony*. Against the southeast wall are two long unlocked chests, with wall shelves filled with candles above them, and a narrow wooden table between them holding three [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment") and an [elven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger").

In the northern corner of the lower level are several sets of shelves, which hold:

:   **Ingredients** (one sample, unless otherwise noted)

:   |  |  |  |  |  |  |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | - [Bear Claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Claws "Skyrim:Bear Claws") - [Bee](/wiki/Skyrim:Bee "Skyrim:Bee") - [Berit's Ashes](/wiki/Skyrim:Berit%27s_Ashes "Skyrim:Berit's Ashes")† - [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") (two)† | - [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") - [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") - [Dwarven Oil](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Oil "Skyrim:Dwarven Oil") - [Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") | - [Falmer Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear") - [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") - [Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") - [Grass Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") | - [Hagraven Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw") - [Hawk Feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers") - [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") - [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") | - [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") - [River Betty](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Betty "Skyrim:River Betty") - [Skeever Tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail") - [Slaughterfish Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales") | - [Spider Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg") - [Swamp Fungal Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod") - [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") - [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") (two) |

† These are a unique bone meal, and can be used to create potions with the same effects as regular bone meal. Version 1.1 of the [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch") replaces them with regular bone meal, raising the total to three.

In addition, there is a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") skill book *[De Rerum Dirennis](/wiki/Skyrim:De_Rerum_Dirennis "Skyrim:De Rerum Dirennis")* on one of the shelves. In the eastern corner between the upper level and the stairs are more sets of shelves holding mostly clutter, two lockpicks, and a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")*.

The balcony overlooking the closed portal

The stairs up to the upper level pass two small wardrobes containing a selection of fine clothes and boots, with two empty [black soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), an empty and a filled [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"), an empty [grand soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Grand Soul Gem"), and six soul gem fragments on top. Also on top and not to be confused with normal soul gem fragments is a stone bowl containing [soul gem shards](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Shards "Skyrim:Soul Gem Shards"), which are needed to create a portal to the Soul Cairn.

At the top of the upper level, in the eastern corner is an alchemy lab, with a narrow table, a set of shelves, and a long table to the left along the northeast wall. In the northern corner is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). In the northwest are stairs up to a balcony featuring six more sets of shelves. The shelves, tables, and alchemy lab hold the following ingredients:

:   **Ingredients** (one sample, unless otherwise noted)

:   |  |  |  |  |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | - [Abecean Longfin](/wiki/Skyrim:Abecean_Longfin "Skyrim:Abecean Longfin") (three) - [Blue Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing") - [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") - [Charred Skeever Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") - [Chicken's Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") - [Creep Cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster") (two) - [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") - [Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") | - [Eye of Sabre Cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Eye_of_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Eye of Sabre Cat") - [Falmer Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear") (two) - [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") (three) - [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") - [Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") (two) - [Garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") - [Ice Wraith Teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth") - [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") | - [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") - [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") - [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") - [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") - [Orange Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") - [Pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl "Skyrim:Pearl") - [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") - [River Betty](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Betty "Skyrim:River Betty") | - [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") (two) - [Skeever Tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail") - [Slaughterfish Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") - [Small Pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Pearl "Skyrim:Small Pearl") - [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") - [Vampire Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust") - [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") - [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") |

In addition to these ingredients, there is a stone bowl containing a sample of [purified void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Purified_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Purified Void Salts"), which are not an ingredient, but will be found under the miscellaneous section of your character's inventory menu, and are needed to create a portal to the Soul Cairn. There is also a random potion or poison on top of the alchemy lab, and another on one of the long tables, with a [potion of blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Blood "Skyrim:Potion of Blood") added to the table after Valerica returns and takes up residence in the castle.

The open portal to the Soul Cairn

A central balcony overlooks the portal area. The balcony lacks a railing along the front, and features a "portal vessel", which is where the three unique items needed to open the portal to the Soul Cairn are placed during the related quest. Once the portal is open, stairs will lead down from this balcony to the portal in the center of the lower area. The portal will remain open permanently.

## Notes

- Although technically in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), anything you steal from the castle doesn't count towards completing a [bedlam job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bedlam_Job "Skyrim:The Bedlam Job") for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
- The room with the three gargoyles in Volkihar Ruins is one of the few places where the vampire royal armor can be obtained, and the only one that respawns.
- Valerica's Study is the only location in the game where you can acquire a dragon bone without defeating a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon").
- Environmental music won't play on the island. Using [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") here will clear away the fog and snow, replacing them with sunny weather.
- After completing Dawnguard's main questline on the Volkihar side, it is possible to repair the path to Volkihar Courtyard from within Volkihar Keep by talking to [Garan Marethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Garan_Marethi "Skyrim:Garan Marethi"). This repair is free of charge, and adds a convenient entrance door to the Courtyard for quicker access to all dungeon locations.
- If the Dawnguard eradicate the vampires who control the castle, picking up any items in Volkihar Keep will still count as [stealing](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime").
- You can exit the laboratory through a door in the southern corner. This leads to the *Castle Volkihar Balcony*, a small outside area from which you can fast-travel and then return to the Soul Cairn without having to traverse the castle ruins and courtyard again. A foot chest near the door also provides easy access to a container to stash loot while fast-travelling. Castle Volkihar Balcony uses the same map icon as [Nordic Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Towers "Skyrim:Towers").
  - If playing on [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") (which disables fast travel), the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") Shout can allow the balcony exit to remain a shortcut outside by jumping off the ledge. Otherwise you'll have to backtrack through the dungeons to go back outside.
- Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch") adds pullchains to allow access to the portcullises in the Volkihar Ruins chapel area, another pullchain to allow access from inside the Volkihar Ruins kitchen area to the Courtyard exit, and switches to allow access from the Volkihar Undercroft across the double bridge on the Courtyard side, if the bridge is raised from there.
- The display case with the Ring of Remedy, Hagraven Claw, Daedra Heart, Eye of Sabrecat, and Dog Meat is a reference to each of Dracula's Relics from the Castlevania games.

## Bugs

- If you return to Volkihar Ruins via the courtyard entrance and pull the first chain again, the door will close, with no way of reopening it except by reloading a previous save or exiting/entering the area.
- Followers are not able to enter the East Tower or North Tower due to unfinished navmeshes.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- Two fireplaces and a portcullis lack proper script properties to allow them to be opened and closed more than once.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- The animated castle fireplace here may have an issue with the collision that can prevent you from passing through it. This would in turn block progress through the Dawnguard questline.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, fixes this bug.
- In the Undercroft is an open coffin containing a coin purse that you may be unable to interact with.
  - Using the console command `tcl` enables you to reach the coin purse.
- When a gargoyle comes to life, there is the sound of an explosion, and chunks of stone fly into the air from where the gargoyle is sitting and land in front of it. If you have already completed the quest [Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes"), and you reenter Castle Volkihar before everything respawns (perhaps to revisit the Soul Cairn), the explosion sound and flying stone chunks will happen again when you approach the places where the gargoyles used to be, despite the fact that they are no longer present. This does not affect anything else, but it may be surprising when it first happens.
- If you are revisiting the dungeon after completing the quest Chasing Echoes, when you enter the Undercroft, it is quite possible that Serana may magically appear as a follower. Be aware that if she does, and you use the dialogue option "Wait here", you will not subsequently be able to issue the command "Follow me". It will not appear as a dialogue option, and she will be left permanently wherever you told her to wait unless you reload a previous save game. **?**
- Although the Dawnguard waiting at the travel spawn point will be immediately hostile upon detecting you, killing them may count as murder and may result in a bounty.
- Although the Castle is (ostensibly) within Haafingar Hold, crimes committed here may earn a bounty in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").
- If you fast travel to the island the castle is on with [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere"), the horse will remain there when you leave. **?**
  - Either mount Shadowmere and fast travel away from the island, or swim to the mainland.

# Skyrim:Castles

## Overview

The Blue Palace in Solitude

This page lists all the **castles** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:    **[Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace")** — The current seat of power for Solitude, Haafingar, and Skyrim; and home to the High King of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blue+Palace)
:   **[Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour")** — A large fortress in Solitude which acts as the headquarters of the Imperial Legion and residence of the Emperor in Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Dour)
:    **[Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large castle on an island far northwest of Solitude connected to Volkihar Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)

    :    **[Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large fortress on an island far northwest of Solitude connected to Castle Volkihar which serves as the Volkihar vampire clan's home. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)
:    **[Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach")** — The residence of the Jarl of Whiterun Hold, the hold's seat of political power, and the location of the hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragonsreach)
:    **[Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim "Skyrim:Hendraheim") — A Nordic hall player home in the Reach, north of Bilegulch Mine. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hendraheim+%28CC%29)
:   **[Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall")** — The residence of Idgrod Ravencrone, the Jarl of Hjaalmarch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Highmoon+Hall)
:   **[Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)")** — The seat of Falkreath's government and home to its jarl. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jarl%27s+Longhouse+%28Falkreath%29)
:   **[Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)")** — A large two-story house in Winterhold, and the court of the city's Jarl. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jarl%27s+Longhouse+%28Winterhold%29)
:    **[Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep")** — A castle located at the southern end of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistveil+Keep)
:    **[Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings")** — A large castle at the far end of the Valunstrad district in Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Palace+of+the+Kings)
:   **[The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall")** — A large two-story structure that sits on a hillside overlooking most of Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+White+Hall)
:    **[Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep")** — An ancient Dwarven keep built into the mountainside, used as a palace by the Jarl of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Understone+Keep)

# Skyrim:Catch of the Day

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Catch fair weather fish.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water") |
| Location(s): | [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") |
| Reward: | 200 Gold |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ1 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Angler Acquaintances](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler_Acquaintances "Skyrim:Angler Acquaintances") | **Next →** [Caught in the Rain](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_the_Rain "Skyrim:Caught in the Rain") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Angler Acquaintances](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler_Acquaintances "Skyrim:Angler Acquaintances") | | → Next | [Caught in the Rain](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_the_Rain "Skyrim:Caught in the Rain") | | |

Catch of the Day

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to Swims-In-Deep-Water inside the Riften Fishery.
2. Read the book in the back room of the Fishery for the optional objective.
3. Go outside the Fishery and at the end of the dock is a Rod and Fishing Supplies where you can catch the list of fish.
4. Return to Swims-In-Deep-Water.

## Detailed Walkthrough

To begin this quest you need to speak to [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water"):

:   **I'd like to improve my fishing skills. Could you teach me a few things?**
:   *"Of course."*
:   **An entire list of fish to catch? But I only just learned how to fish!**
:   *"That doesn't change anything."*

You then have three options:

:   **Should I cook them for you while I'm at it?**

    :   *"What? Nooo!"*

        :   **Relax, I was just joking.**
        :   *"You expect me to believe that?"*

            :   **The fish you tend to at the Fishery must be very important to you.**
            :   *"It speaks the truth."*

:   **I'll bring them back soon.**

    :   *"My thanks to you."*

:   **I'll do my best. No promises.**

    :   *"Of course."*

He will hand you a [list of fair weather fish](/wiki/Skyrim:List_of_Fair_Weather_Fish "Skyrim:List of Fair Weather Fish"), which requests you to catch:

- [Carp](/wiki/Skyrim:Carp "Skyrim:Carp")
- [Glassfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Glassfish "Skyrim:Glassfish")
- [Goldfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldfish "Skyrim:Goldfish")
- [Pogfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Pogfish "Skyrim:Pogfish")

You can find a copy of *[Fishing Mastery, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Mastery,_v1 "Skyrim:Fishing Mastery, v1")* on a shelf in the room behind Swims. This book will inform you of where you can catch each of these fish. All of the fish can be found in temperate lakes and rivers, see [this link](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Fishing_Locations "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") for a list of fishing locations, but these fish can all be caught in the docks of Riften and along the river that leads to Ivarstead.

Once you have caught all the fish required, return to Swims:

:   **Here are the fish you asked for.**
:   *"You've done well."*

He will then reward you with 200 gold.

## Quest Stages

| Catch of the Day (ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ1) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Swims-In-Deep-Water has given me a list of fish I should catch to improve my fishing skills. I should read the note to see what I need to catch. *Objective :* Read the list of fair weather fish |
| 20 |  | Swims-In-Deep-Water would like me to catch fish that can commonly be caught in streams and lakes in the warmer parts of Skyrim. Once I've caught one of each, I should return them to him. His field guide, Fishing Mastery, should provide details on each fish and how they can be caught. He mentioned that a copy is sitting on a shelf in the back room of the Riften Fishery. *Objective 0:* Obtain a carp  *Objective 1:* Obtain a glassfish  *Objective 2:* Obtain a goldfish  *Objective 3:* Obtain a pogfish  *Objective 75:* (Optional) Read Fishing Mastery, v1 |
| 21 |  | I read the first volume of Fishing Mastery, Swims-In-Deep-Water's field guide. All of the fish I need to catch can be caught in the warmer parts of Skyrim on a clear day. Goldfish and glassfish can only be caught in lakes, while pogfish are found in streams. Carp can be caught in both lakes and streams. I should be able to catch what I need by fishing of off the docks near the Riften Fishery, and along the river that leads to Ivarstead. *Objective 50:* Return to Swims-In-Deep-Water |
| 200 | ☑ | I've given Swims-In-Deep-Water all of the fish he requested as proof of completing his fishing challenge. In return, he gave me a sum of gold, as well as a key to the Riften Fishery. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ1 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ1`.

# Skyrim:Caught in a Web

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Search for legendary artifacts in a spider den.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | *[Adonato Leotelli's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato_Leotelli%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli's Journal")*, [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"), [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| Location(s): | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave") |
| Reward: | [Fists of Randagulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Fists_of_Randagulf "Skyrim:Fists of Randagulf") and [Ice Blade of the Monarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Blade_of_the_Monarch "Skyrim:Ice Blade of the Monarch") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE069\_Quest |
| Added by: | [The Contest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Contest "Skyrim:The Contest") |

Caught in a Web

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read [Adonato Leotelli's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato_Leotelli%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli's Journal") in [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall").
2. Kill the [Web Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Web_Mother "Skyrim:Web Mother") in [Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave").
3. Loot the bodies of [Grenwulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Grenwulf_the_Brawler "Skyrim:Grenwulf the Brawler") and [Holrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Holrik_Frost-Sword "Skyrim:Holrik Frost-Sword").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Success

To start this quest you need to read [Adonato Leotelli's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato_Leotelli%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli's Journal") which can be found on a table on the upper floor of [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"). You will then need to travel to [Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave").

At the end of the lair, the web mother will drop down and attack you alongside some [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). The web mother can spit projectile spiders. The spirits of [Holrik Frost-Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Holrik_Frost-Sword "Skyrim:Holrik Frost-Sword") and [Grenwulf the Brawler](/wiki/Skyrim:Grenwulf_the_Brawler "Skyrim:Grenwulf the Brawler") will join the fight, and once the web mother is dead, will walk to their corpses.

Investigate Holrik's body and you will find the [Ice Blade of the Monarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Blade_of_the_Monarch "Skyrim:Ice Blade of the Monarch") and [Holrik's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Holrik%27s_Note "Skyrim:Holrik's Note"). Investigate Grenwulf's body and you will find the [Fists of Randagulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Fists_of_Randagulf "Skyrim:Fists of Randagulf") and [Grenwulf's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Grenwulf%27s_Note "Skyrim:Grenwulf's Note").

## Notes

- At the bottom of the first large chamber within Cronvangr Cave there is a button that opens to a vampire lair. This is an optional quest overlap location. This is the lair location of one of the "Pets of Skyrim". Behind the gory shack on the upper ledge and in a cage is the Tamable Frostbite spider named "[Arachnia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arachnia "Skyrim:Arachnia")". It can be picked up now or later on following its associated quest.

## Bugs

- Sometimes the quest won't start even after reading Adonato Leotelli's Journal. **?**
  - Manually triggering the quest by using console command `setstage ccBGSSSE069_quest 20` will solve this issue.
- After killing the Web Mother, Grenwulf's ghost may not lead you to his corpse after Holrik has done the same.
  - Exiting the Broodlair into the main cave and returning will remedy this.
  - You can also use `resurrect 0` in the console.
- Grenwulf and Holrik can be given follower commands by holding the action key. Doing that, then waiting for them to disappear and then giving a command to either one will instantly crash the game. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Caught in a Web (ccBGSSSE069\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've heard many great warriors have come through Skyrim over the years, and passed through Candlehearth Hall in Windhelm. If I travel there, I may hear some stories of what became of them. *Objective 10:* Investigate Candlehearth Hall |
| 20 |  | I traveled to Candlehearth Hall and read a journal about two warriors, who traveled to Cronvangr Cave to defeat a dangerous spider. I should travel to the cave and find out what became of them. *Objective 20:* Search Cronvangr Cave for the two heroes |
| 30 |  | I traveled to Candlehearth Hall and read a journal about two warriors, who traveled to Cronvangr Cave to defeat a dangerous spider. I traveled to Cronvangr Cave and found the spider's lair. *Objective 30:* Defeat the Web Mother |
| 40 |  | I traveled to Candlehearth Hall and read a journal about two warriors, who traveled to Cronvangr Cave to defeat a dangerous Web Mother. I traveled to Cronvangr Cave and found the spider's lair, defeating the Web Mother. *Objective 40:* Speak to the Heroes |
| 40 |  | I traveled to Candlehearth Hall and read a journal about two warriors, who traveled to Cronvangr Cave to defeat a dangerous Web Mother. I traveled to Cronvangr Cave and found the spider's lair, defeating the Web Mother. I spoke to the heroes who bequeathed me their treasures before fading away. |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Inspect Grenwulf's corpse |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Inspect Holrik's corpse |
| 100 | ☑ | I traveled to Candlehearth Hall and read a journal about two warriors, who traveled to Cronvangr Cave to defeat a dangerous Web Mother. I traveled to Cronvangr Cave and found the spider's lair, defeating the Web Mother. After the battle, the heroes rewarded me with their treasures. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 15.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE069_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE069_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Caught in the Rain

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Catch rainy weather fish.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water") |
| Location(s): | [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery"), West of [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm") |
| Reward: | [Argonian Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Argonian Fishing Rod"), 400 Gold |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ2 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Catch of the Day](/wiki/Skyrim:Catch_of_the_Day "Skyrim:Catch of the Day") | **Next →** [Frozen Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Fish "Skyrim:Frozen Fish") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Catch of the Day](/wiki/Skyrim:Catch_of_the_Day "Skyrim:Catch of the Day") | | → Next | [Frozen Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Fish "Skyrim:Frozen Fish") | | |

Caught in the Rain

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") and speak with [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water").
2. Read [List of Rainy Weather Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:List_of_Rainy_Weather_Fish "Skyrim:List of Rainy Weather Fish").
3. (Optional) Read [Fishing Mastery, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Mastery,_v2 "Skyrim:Fishing Mastery, v2").
4. Obtain a [Catfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Catfish "Skyrim:Catfish").
5. Obtain a [Pearlfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearlfish "Skyrim:Pearlfish").
6. Obtain a [Pygmy Sunfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Pygmy_Sunfish "Skyrim:Pygmy Sunfish").
7. Obtain a [Spadefish](/wiki/Skyrim:Spadefish "Skyrim:Spadefish").
8. Obtain Swims-In-Deep-Water's [Lucky Fishing Hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucky_Fishing_Hat "Skyrim:Lucky Fishing Hat").
9. Hand your fish over to Swims-In-Deep-Water and decide on whether to keep the Lucky Fishing Hat or give it back.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The fishing camp at Geirmund's Hall

Speak to Swims for this next challenge:

:   **I'm ready for the next fishing challenge.**
:   *"It's all in this note."*
:   **I see, these fish come out in the rain. And... you lost your lucky fishing hat?**
:   *"It speaks the truth."*

:   :   **Alright. I'll be back soon with the fish. And the hat.**
    :   *"My thanks to you."*

:   :   **I'll get started. I just wish I didn't have to get soaked.**
    :   *"My thanks to you."*

Fish tank after completion of the quest

He then hands you a [list of rainy weather fish](/wiki/Skyrim:List_of_Rainy_Weather_Fish "Skyrim:List of Rainy Weather Fish"), which tells you that you need to catch a:

- [Catfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Catfish "Skyrim:Catfish")
- [Pearlfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearlfish "Skyrim:Pearlfish")
- [Pygmy Sunfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Pygmy_Sunfish "Skyrim:Pygmy Sunfish")
- [Spadefish](/wiki/Skyrim:Spadefish "Skyrim:Spadefish")

You can also optionally pickup a copy of [Fishing Mastery, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Mastery,_v2 "Skyrim:Fishing Mastery, v2") from the shelf in the backroom. Travel to [Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall"), where you can fish up Swims' lucky fishing hat, which when worn will cause thunderstorms while fishing at temperate lakes and streams, making this quest much easier.

Once you have caught the required fish, return to Swims where you can either return his hat to him or lie that you didn't find it:

:   :   **Here are the fish you were after. I also found your lucky fishing hat.**
    :   *"You are like my brood to me. Here. A token."*

:   :   **Here's the fish for the challenge. I couldn't find your lucky fishing hat. (Lie)**
    :   *"It can't be helped. Thank you. Here this is for you."*

Either option leads to you getting an Argonian fishing rod and the ability to create more, if you give Swims his hat back, he will also reward you with 400 gold:

:   **Thanks for the Argonian fishing rod, and the coin. I'll put them to good use.**
:   **An Argonian fishing rod? Thank you. I will be sure to put it to good use.**
:   *"My thanks to you."*

## Bugs

- The journal states that you can find pygmy sunfish in streams, when in reality they are found in lakes when it is raining.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130.0, fixes this bug.
- The objective to "Fish up Swims-In-Deep-Water's lucky fishing hat" and a quest marker to the respective fishing spot appear right after the quest is given, but the [Lucky Fishing Hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucky_Fishing_Hat "Skyrim:Lucky Fishing Hat") can only be fished after the *[List of Rainy Weather Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:List_of_Rainy_Weather_Fish "Skyrim:List of Rainy Weather Fish")* is read.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. The objective for fishing up the hat will no longer be displayed until after the note is read.
- The fish tank that's supposed to receive the fish you turn in during the quest was never properly set in the script properties, which can lead to the fish not being added to it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 4.3.3, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Caught in the Rain (ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ2) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Swims-In-Deep-Water has given me another fishing challenge. I should read the list he gave me to see what I will need to catch. *Objective 100:* Read the list of rainy weather fish  *Objective 10:* Fish up Swims-In-Deep-Water's lucky fishing hat |
| 20 |  | The fish that Swims-In-Deep-Water would like me to catch are a bit more elusive than last time. However, they come to the surface more frequently while it is raining. I should refer to the second volume of Fishing Mastery to learn more. He also asked me to help fish up his lucky fishing hat, lost at a fishing spot west of Sarethi Farm. He claims that it rains wherever he wears the hat when fishing. That sounds far-fetched, but I suppose I could use all the luck I can get. *Objective 0:* Obtain a catfish  *Objective 1:* Obtain a pearlfish  *Objective 2:* Obtain a pygmy sunfish  *Objective 3:* Obtain a spadefish  *Objective 75:* (Optional) Read Fishing Mastery, v2 |
| 21 |  | I have read the second volume of Fishing Mastery. All of the fish I need to catch are most easily caught when it's raining in the warmer parts of Skyrim. Catfish and spadefish can only be caught in lakes, while pygmy sunfish are found in streams. Pearlfish can be caught in both lakes and streams. He also asked me to help fish up his lucky fishing hat, lost at a fishing spot west of Sarethi Farm. He claims that it rains wherever he wears the hat when fishing. That sounds far-fetched, but I suppose I could use all the luck I can get. *Objective 50:* Return to Swims-In-Deep-Water |
| 200 | ☑ | I've given Swims-In-Deep-Water all of the fish he requested as proof of completing his fishing challenge, as well as his lucky fishing hat. He rewarded me with an Argonian fishing rod, which will be useful when trying to catch large fish. He also handed me a sum of gold. |
| 210 | ☑ | I've given Swims-In-Deep-Water all of the fish he requested as proof of completing his fishing challenge. I kept his lucky fishing hat to myself after telling him I couldn't find it. He rewarded me with an Argonian fishing rod, which will be useful when trying to catch large fish. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 30, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ2`.
