# Skyrim:Caught Red Handed

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Gather three marks of Dibella to help [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") against [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") |
| Location(s): | [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse") |
| Reward: | Enchanted Heavy Armor, Leveled Scroll |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften11 |

*"My dear aunt, I'm ready to catch you."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") in [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse").
2. Obtain the [Marks of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mark_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Mark of Dibella") from [Bolli](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli "Skyrim:Bolli"), [Indaryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Indaryn "Skyrim:Indaryn"), and [Hofgrir](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher").
3. Confront [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga").
4. Return to Svana.

### A Worshipper

If you visit [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), you may see [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") busy doing some cleaning there. The work is difficult and endless, and she prefers to call it slavery. Ever since her parents died and [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga") took her in, it's been a nightmare. She was surprised to learn that Haelga is such a wretched woman. *"So now I'm stuck living here while those pigs she calls customers grope me and say the most awful things."* In her opinion, Haelga is disgusting and she takes her worship of [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella") a bit too seriously. According to Svana, Haelga slept with three different men in the last month. Svana would like to see her squirm just once. She happens to know that after Haelga makes love, she gives her partner a token of her affection called a [Mark of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mark_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Mark of Dibella"). If you collect the marks from [Bolli](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli "Skyrim:Bolli"), [Indaryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Indaryn "Skyrim:Indaryn"), and [Hofgrir](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") (All three men are located in Riften), and confront Haelga with them, it would cause her endless embarrassment. Furthermore, Svana asks that you collect the marks without violence.

### Three Lovers

In order to get the three Marks of Dibella, you can use your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skills to persuade or intimidate the men into giving their marks to you. Alternatively, you can just [pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") the marks from your targets. If you kill any of the men, the quest will fail immediately.

[Bolli](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli "Skyrim:Bolli") can usually be found wandering in the market or working in [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery"). Talk to him about the mark and he will say *"I have no idea what you're talking about. I'd never sleep with anyone besides my good wife, Drifa*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*."* You must pass an average-level [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him.

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Hand it over and no one has to know.  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Look, it was one night, okay? I think she slipped something in my drink. I haven't even been back to the Bunkhouse since. Just take this damn thing. I never want to see it again. **Failed**: Hand what over? I have no idea what you're talking about. | **Passed**: Get the Mark of Dibella **Failed**: Nothing |
| Give it to me or else!  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Look, it was one night, okay? I think she slipped something in my drink. I haven't even been back to the Bunkhouse since. Just take this damn thing. I never want to see it again. **Failed**: Or else what? You don't scare me. | **Passed**: Get the Mark of Dibella **Failed**: Nothing |
| Never mind. My mistake. | I should say so. | Nothing |

[Indaryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Indaryn "Skyrim:Indaryn") can usually be found at the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery"), but he will visit [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") too. If you talk to him about Haelga, he will be a little angry *"You're crazy! How dare you make such an accusation!"* You must pass an average-level [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him.

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Hand it over and no one has to know.  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: If word gets around that I bedded her, they'll lose all respect for me at the meadery. Take the mark if you want it. It's not worth all this hassle anyway. **Failed**: You aren't making any sense. Hand what over? | **Passed**: Get the Mark of Dibella **Failed**: Nothing |
| Give it to me or else!  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: If word gets around that I bedded her, they'll lose all respect for me at the meadery. Take the mark if you want it. It's not worth all this hassle anyway. **Failed**: You're threatening me? Oh, that's rich! | **Passed**: Get the Mark of Dibella **Failed**: Nothing |
| Never mind. My mistake. | You've got some nerve. | Nothing |

[Hofgrir](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") is the owner of the [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables") and you can find him there easily. If you ask him to give you the mark, he will pretend to be innocent: *"Huh? What are you talking about? I don't even know what that is."* You must pass an easy-level [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him. (See [Bugs](#Bugs)).

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Hand it over and no one has to know.  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: I don't want a bad reputation in Riften, but Haelga's out of control. She wanted to try it in the stables so I said yes. If you want the mark that badly then go ahead and take it. **Failed**: Look, you must have me confused with someone else. | **Passed**: Get the Mark of Dibella **Failed**: Nothing |
| Give it to me or else!  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: I don't want a bad reputation in Riften, but Haelga's out of control. She wanted to try it in the stables so I said yes. If you want the mark that badly then go ahead and take it. **Failed**: You have a death wish or something? | **Passed**: Get the Mark of Dibella **Failed**: Nothing |
| Never mind. My mistake. | Next time think before you speak. | Nothing |

### Two Rewards

Once you have all three Marks of Dibella, return to Haelga's Bunkhouse and show them to Haelga. She will be surprised. *"What? How... where did you get these?"* Obviously, she doesn't want anyone else to know about it, especially Svana. She will give you a [magic scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls") to keep you quiet. *"If word got out that I'm practicing my Dibellan Arts in Riften, they'll run me out of town."*

Bring the news to Svana, and she will be quite happy. *"Oh I know. Isn't it wonderful? I bet she squirmed like a skeever when you pulled them out of your pocket."* She believes things are going to be a lot different around here with your help. Then she will give you a piece of enchanted armor in return. *"I want you to have this. It was my father's but I'm certain you'll put it to good use."*

## Notes

- [Blessing of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Blessing of Dibella") (+10 Speechcraft for 8 hours) from the shrine in Haelga's bedroom and [Gift of Charity](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gift_of_Charity "Skyrim:The Gift of Charity") (+10 Speechcraft for 1 hour) from giving alms to [Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Edda "Skyrim:Edda") or [Snilf](/wiki/Skyrim:Snilf "Skyrim:Snilf") can improve your chance to persuade targets to hand over marks of Dibella.
- After you complete this quest, you will be allowed to take low value items from anywhere in [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse") (due to your new friendship with Svana), even items found in her boarders' containers.
- Svana will not offer the quest if one of the three lovers was already killed before talking to her.

## Bugs

- If you have pickpocketed any of the marks of Dibella by accident before receiving the quest, make sure to find all three before attempting to speak to anyone. You will get a notice to confront Haelga in your miscellaneous quest log. You can talk to Haelga and Svana without the requisite dialogue options and then talk to Haelga again. You will get to give the stones to Haelga after all and your quest will complete and a reward given.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- After acquiring one of the marks before ever picking up the quest, Svana will urge you to find the rest of the marks though you won't see anything in your quest log. However after obtaining all three, a miscellaneous objective to confront Haelga will then appear and the quest can be taken through to completion from that point on with items received from both Haelga and Svana.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- When asking Bolli about his relationship with Haelga he will remark that he has never slept with any woman other than his wife [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa"). However, Bolli's wife is [Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- Hofgrir Horse-Crusher's persuade check is incorrectly flagged to check his Speech level rather than yours.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Hofgrir's intimidation check can be used, instead, which always works.

## Quest Stages

| Caught Red Handed (FreeformRiften11) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Obtain a Mark of Dibella from Bolli  *Objective 20:* Obtain a Mark of Dibella from Hofgrir  *Objective 30:* Obtain a Mark of Dibella from Indaryn |
| 60 |  | *Objective 40:* Confront Haelga with the Marks of Dibella |
| 70 |  | *Objective 50:* Speak to Svana |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 30, 40, 50, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften11 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften11`.

# Skyrim:Caves

## Overview

Cragwallow Slope

 This page lists all the **caves** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:    **[Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") — A small cave north of Raven Rock containing a hidden Tribunal Temple shrine to the goddess Almalexia. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ashfall%27s+Tear+%28CC%29)
:    **[Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A medium-sized cave southeast of Saering's Watch containing bristlebacks and rieklings. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Benkongerike)
:   **[Blackbone Isle Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle_Grotto "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle Grotto")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") — A small cave connected to the sea, situated on Blackbone Isle. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackbone+Isle+Grotto)
:    **[Bleakcoast Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakcoast_Cave "Skyrim:Bleakcoast Cave")** — A small cave east-southeast of Winterhold containing frost trolls. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakcoast+Cave)
:    **[Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave")** — A medium-sized cave southwest of Karthwasten along the banks of the Karth River containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
:    **[Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto")** — A small cave north of Falkreath containing animals and spriggans. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloated+Man%27s+Grotto)
:    **[Bloodchill Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Cavern "Skyrim:Bloodchill Cavern")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor") — A small cave southwest of Winterhold containing a subterranean vampiric player home. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloodchill+Cavern+%28CC%29)
:    **[Bonechill Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonechill_Passage "Skyrim:Bonechill Passage")** — A small cave east of Falkreath containing leveled animals. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bonechill+Passage)
:    **[Boulderfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Boulderfall_Cave "Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave")** — A small cave northwest of Riften containing necromancers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Boulderfall+Cave)
:    **[Brinewater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Brinewater_Grotto "Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto")** — A small cave north of Solitude containing horkers or bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brinewater+Grotto)
:    **[Bristleback Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback_Cave "Skyrim:Bristleback Cave")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small cave in the northwest of Solstheim island containing bristlebacks and rieklings. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Bristleback+Cave)
:    **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small passage through the mountains between Whiterun Hold and Falkreath Hold containing a necromancer and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)

## Notes

- Version 2.0.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces Yngvild's cave map icon with the one used for [Nordic ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins").
- Version 3.0.6 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch") replaces the cave map icon for Soljund's Sinkhole with the one used for [mines](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines").

Cedran

**Cedran** is the [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") hostler at [Markarth Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Stables "Skyrim:Markarth Stables"). He can sell you a black and white [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") for 1000 septims.

He wears farmer's [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothing"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209a5 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000209aa "Skyrim:Clothing"). He carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Markarth_Stables "Skyrim:Key to Markarth Stables") to Markarth Stables.

He wakes up in the stables at 8am, and gets to work at the stables right away. After working the stables for twelve hours straight, he'll head back inside, at 8pm. He'll then relax inside for four hours, before going to bed at midnight.

## Related Quests

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

When you greet him, he can say:

:   *"You need a reliable horse in the Reach. That's what we have."*
:   *"You treat a horse well, it'll take you to Oblivion and back."*

If his assistant, [Banning](/wiki/Skyrim:Banning "Skyrim:Banning"), is dead, he'll say:

:   *"Poor Banning. Twice as much work here in the stables without him."*

If spoken to directly he can be asked questions about the area:

:   **Who's in charge of Markarth?**
:   *"That would be [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"). Young for a ruler of a Hold, especially the Reach. Wasn't surprising he stayed loyal to the Empire. His father helped capture Ulfric Stormcloak after the Markarth incident."* **(Imperials control Markarth)**

:   *"Since the Stormcloaks took over, Jarl [Thongvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood") is in charge. It'll be lean times for [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") with a Silver-Blood ruling it, that's for certain."* **(Stormcloaks control Markarth)**

:   **What's the Markarth Incident?**
:   *"It's the whole reason Ulfric revolted against the Empire. Well, the first reason anyway. Forsworn had taken over Markarth, and Ulfric and his men drove them out. Empire promised they'd be free to worship Talos afterwards. Pity no one told the Elves. Whole group of those Thalmor came and they demanded Ulfric's arrest."*

:   **Who are the Forsworn?**
:   *"Before the Nords came, we worshipped the old gods, had our own kingdom. Times have been good and bad since then, but some folks couldn't handle not ruling their own land. Those are the Forsworn. The Forsworn follow the old ways, but some of those were best forgotten. Blood sacrifices, communing with Daedra. It's the road to ruin."*

When exiting conversation, he can say:

:   *"May the crags fail to trip your feet."*
:   *"Safe travels to you."*

## Conversations

He can sometimes be seen conversing with Banning:

:   **Cedran**: *"Think we should buy more horses next season?"*
:   **Banning**: *"I'd rather spend the gold on a new litter of pups, but the horses bring in more gold."*

:   **Banning**: *"How are the new breeds getting along with my dogs?"*
:   **Cedran**: *"Haven't attacked each other yet. Good a sign as any."*

## Unused Dialogue

Cedran was at one point meant to have a minor role in [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy"). Although unknown what would be the starting point, you could come and ask him about a possible Forsworn escape plan. This dialogue can only be found in the game's DialogueViews files, and not the Creation Kit.

:   **I need to know if [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach") ever came to you about getting horses.**
:   *"Madanach? Haven't heard that name is a long while. Yeah, he asked, but I told that old Forsworn he could walk out of the city if he ever managed to break out of that prison. Don't like the Nords any more than he does, but I don't help criminals. Plain and simple."*

## Notes

- Cedran was at one point meant to be the local bard of the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn"). His class is a remnant of this, and he is still internally marked as an employee of both [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr") and [Frabbi](/wiki/Skyrim:Frabbi "Skyrim:Frabbi"). It seems that he was meant to have a particular strong bond with their daughter, [Hroki](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroki "Skyrim:Hroki"), as they have relationship rank of "Ally" and he is marked as her master with her being his assistant.
  - Cedran is also marked as a friend of [Eltrys](/wiki/Skyrim:Eltrys "Skyrim:Eltrys"), but neither man ever acknowledges each other's existence in the final game. It's possible that this relation is tied to the unused portion of The Forsworn Conspiracy, as seen above.

Celann

**Celann** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") and [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") hunter who can be found at [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"). Like Dawnguard leader [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran"), Celann is a former [Vigilant of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr"), but they both left due to dissatisfaction with the organization. Later on, they parted ways, but naturally Celann was one of the first warriors to be offered a place in Isran's newly formed [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). Once the quest [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") has been completed, Celann will also be available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") but will keep up his daily routine.

Once Awakening has been started Celann will start his regular routine. He owns one of the cots in the northern section on the ground floor and sleeps there between 8pm and 4am. After he wakes up he walks over to the western dining area where he hangs out all day long, eating, relaxing, or wandering around. However, during the quest [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order"), when you return to the fort after visiting [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep") with [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana"), you will find Celann, Isran, and [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak") fighting off an attack by vampires just outside the gate. After the battle, Celann will retake his position outside the gate, ready to protect the fort. He will stay put until you bring the reinforcements, [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard") and [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar").

He is clad in a set of Dawnguard light equipment. This includes the gray [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Armor "Skyrim:Dawnguard Armor") as well as matching pairs of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dawnguard Gauntlets") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Boots "Skyrim:Dawnguard Boots"). He is equipped with a [Dawnguard war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard War Axe") and carries a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"). He knows the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") spell [Sun Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Fire "Skyrim:Sun Fire").

## Related Quests

- **[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)")**: Speak with the leader of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**: Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment")**: Confront [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon").
- **[Destroying the Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroying_the_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Destroying the Dawnguard")**: Kill the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") leaders.

### Dawnguard

When you arrive at the gate of Fort Dawnguard for the first time, along with newcomer [Agmaer](/wiki/Skyrim:Agmaer "Skyrim:Agmaer"), you will find Celann guarding the gate, saying:

:   *"New recruits? Hmm."*
:   *"Here to join the Dawnguard? Good."*
:   *"Isran will decide if you've got what it takes. Go on, he's right inside."*

When you speak to him he will immediately share his concerns:

:   *"I'll tell you, the only thing more surprising than hearing from Isran after all these years was hearing that he wanted my help. I immediately realized things must be pretty bad. Looks like I was right."*
:   **You've worked with Isran before?**
:   *"I have. There was a time, years ago, when we were both members of the Vigilants, and both equally dissatisfied with them. Their hearts are in the right place, of course. But Isran and I were never comfortable. We left together, but that partnership didn't last very long. I didn't agree with some of his methods."*

He will finish the conversation with encouragement:

:   *"Go on inside. Isran'll want to talk to you."*
:   *"May you always prevail."*

### Awakening

When you return to him after Isran's given you the quest [Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening"), he will joyfully remark:

:   *"Isran found something for you to do, eh? I thought he'd like you. Good luck!"*

### Kindred Judgment

When it is time to confront [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") during the quest [Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment"), Celann will listen to Isran's speech in the main hall along with the other Dawnguard members. When Isran gives the order, Celann travels halfway across [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to Castle Volkihar and will participate in the joint effort to kill all residing vampires, while shouting:

:   *"Kill the abominations!"*

When all is said and done, he will sheathe his weapon and walk all the way back to Fort Dawnguard and live there indefinitely with the other members.

## Unused Scenes

In an earlier iteration of [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order"), you were originally meant to start out at [Stendarr's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Stendarr's Beacon"). Here, a meeting between [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") and [Vigilant Tolan](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Tolan "Skyrim:Vigilant Tolan") would have taken place. At some unknown point after this, you would've been sent to Fort Dawnguard for the very first time, where you would've been greeted by this scene between Celann and [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak"):

:   **Durak:** *"Here comes another one!"*
:   **Celann:** *"Hold it! She's/He's the one Tolan mentioned."*
:   **Durak:** *"Ugh. I thought this place was supposed to be secret?"*
:   **Celann:** *"Well it was... Thank the Vigilants for ruining that."*

## Notes

- Celann is one of few followers who have no level cap. He will continue to level up with you.

## Bugs

- Celann is equipped with a set of light armor despite being more proficient in [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. He has been equipped with a set of heavy Dawnguard armor.
- Celann has the [Custom Fit](/wiki/Skyrim:Custom_Fit "Skyrim:Custom Fit") perk even though he is more proficient in Heavy Armor.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, addresses this issue. He has been given the [Well Fitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Fitted "Skyrim:Well Fitted") perk instead.
- During Kindred Judgment and/or Destroying the Dawnguard, Celann may be given 15 crossbows in his inventory, which is clearly an error as it was a copypasta matching the amount of steel bolts he's given.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
- He has the [Champion's Stance](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Stance "Skyrim:Champion's Stance") perk even though he is more proficient in [one-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") weapons (and has 3 perks for them).

Celeste

Celeste is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") leader of the [Blackwater Brigands](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackwater_Brigands "Skyrim:Blackwater Brigands"), and carries the [Blackwater Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackwater_Blade "Skyrim:Blackwater Blade") artifact.

## Related Quests

- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

## Bugs

- Celeste doesn't drop the artifact if she is killed before the quest objective sends you to her. **?**

# Skyrim:Cemeteries

## Overview

Hall of the Dead in Solitude

This page lists all the named **cemeteries** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:   **[Hall of the Dead (Falkreath)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Falkreath)")** — Both Falkreath's only temple and home for both Runil, the priest of Arkay, and Kust, who is responsible for looking after Falkreath's cemetery. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Dead+%28Falkreath%29)
:   **[Hall of the Dead (Markarth)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)")** — A large building in Markarth where the corpses of the deceased are laid to rest. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Dead+%28Markarth%29)
:   **[Hall of the Dead (Riften)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)")** — A small gravesite below the Temple of Mara in Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Dead+%28Riften%29)
:   **[Hall of the Dead (Solitude)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)")** — Where Solitude's dead are brought to be prepared for burial. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Dead+%28Solitude%29)
:   **[Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)")** — The final resting place for many of Whiterun's late residents. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Dead+%28Whiterun%29)
:   **[Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)")** — A small gravesite located in the north end of the graveyard in Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Dead+%28Windhelm%29)
:   **[Morvayn Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Morvayn Ancestral Tomb")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A Dunmer ancestral tomb in Raven Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Morvayn+Ancestral+Tomb)
:   **[Temple Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Temple Ancestral Tomb")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A Dunmer ancestral tomb in Raven Rock.
:   **[Ulen Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulen_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Ulen Ancestral Tomb")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A Dunmer ancestral tomb in Raven Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ulen+Ancestral+Tomb)

# Skyrim:Challenger

## Overview

| Challenger | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |

The Challenger

The **Challenger** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") who is [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#WIChangeLocation03 "Skyrim:World Interactions") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)") (or [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")). He wears [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor") and a leveled pair of [light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and he carries a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), along with various [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), and other items depending on his level.

## Related Quests

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:Wizard Duel")**: Fend off and defeat a challenger. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Wizard Duel

When you first encounter him, he will call out to you:

:   *"You call yourself a wizard? I challenge you to a duel!"*

:   :   **Sorry. You'll have to find some other way to stroke your ego.**
    :   *"I won't take no for answer!"*

:   :   **It's your funeral.**
    :   *"The gods will be the judge of that."*

Either way, you're in for a fight.

He expects you to use magic, and if you don't follow his assumed rules of the duel, he may react with these lines:

:   *"Stop it! This is a one-on-one duel!"*
:   *"I thought you were a wizard. Hit me with a spell!"*
:   *"You're cheating!"*
:   *"It's no fun unless you fight me with magic."*
:   *"This is a magic duel. Ma-gic. You know, with spells."*

# Skyrim:Champion of Boethiah

## Overview

| Champion of Boethiah (RefID: 000834FF) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Knifepoint Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Mine "Skyrim:Knifepoint Mine") | | |

| Level | Radiant (7-51) | Class | [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_(class) "Skyrim:Forsworn (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000834FF | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000834FE |
| Other Information | | | |

| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") | | |

The Champion of Boethiah, wearing the Ebony Mail

The **Champion of Boethiah** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") residing in [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge"). Killing him is the final challenge in [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling"). He is equipped with the [Ebony Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Mail "Skyrim:Ebony Mail"), as well as [ebony boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Boots "Skyrim:Ebony Boots"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Ebony Gauntlets"), and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Shield "Skyrim:Ebony Shield"). He carries a leveled enchanted sword, which can be up to daedric in quality.

## Related Quests

- **[Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling")**: Become [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah")'s new champion.

### Boethiah's Calling

He has unique dialogue explaining why he renounced [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"), but due to his high aggression, you must [calm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(effect) "Skyrim:Pacify (effect)") him in order to hear it.

:   **So you're Boethiah's champion, eh?**
:   *"That was a long time ago."*
:   **Boethiah is displeased. She wants you dead.**
:   *"The Prince of Plots usually gets what she wants. I'm surprised I'm not dead already. She must have had some reason to keep me alive so long."*

:   :   **This is what you want? To slave for others? What about your own destiny?**
    :   *"Mind my words or I'll mind them for you: I'm slave to no man, no god, and no [Daedra](/wiki/Lore:Daedra "Lore:Daedra"). Boethiah talks about leaving your mark, a sign of your passing.... Well, you can make a mark on the world without treachery and murder. Whenever a man's life is saved by armor made with these hands, these hands have changed that man's destiny and his family's. So you can tell that heartless Daedra bitch I'm done doing her dirty work."*

:   :   **You aren't afraid to die?**
    :   *"A man who feels no fear has no heart. I know fear. But it does not control me. If you desire to fight me, then let's get this over with."*

:   :   **Tell me, what's it like being Boethiah's champion?**
    :   *"I told you. I'm done with all that. There's enough blood on these hands. I'm interested in creating things now."*

## Bugs

- The Champion of Boethiah will re-equip his armor if he is killed and revived with [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall"), which can be exploited for infinite gold and powerful armor for your followers.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, addresses this issue. The patch makes him a ghost shortly after Ebony Mail is looted, so he can not be taken away from the cave. There is still a very small time window where he can be reanimated.

Champion's Rest

**Champion's Rest** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") located in [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), east of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). It was once used as a gladiatorial arena but now serves as a crypt for fallen warriors. Once lost to time, miners from Shor's Stone have recently broken through into the ruins while mining for [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver").

It consists of two zones: [Champion's Rest](#Champion.27s_Rest) and [Champion's Rest Amphitheater](#Champion.27s_Rest_Amphitheater).

## Related Quests

- **[Vile Whispers](/wiki/Skyrim:Vile_Whispers "Skyrim:Vile Whispers")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Umbra "Skyrim:Umbra"): A [malevolent Daedric entity](/wiki/Lore:Umbra "Lore:Umbra") long thought destroyed has resurfaced in the [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains").

## Notes

- The boss-level draugr at this location can be a [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") at higher levels.

## Bugs

- This location is marked as undiscovered on your map from the start of the game.

# Skyrim:Chasing Echoes

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Explore [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") |
| Location(s): | [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") |
| Reward: | Entrance to the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") |

| Suggested Level: | 10 |
| Difficulty: | Medium (Vampire Side Only) Hard (Dawnguard Side Only) |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") or [Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)") | **Concurrent** [Seeking Disclosure](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeking_Disclosure "Skyrim:Seeking Disclosure") | **Next →** [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death") | | |

Something is wrong with the moon dial...

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana").
2. Explore [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar").
3. Investigate the Moondial.
4. Explore Castle Volkihar's Ruined Tower.
5. Locate Valerica's Journal.
6. (If not a vampire) Become a [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") or get partially soul trapped.
7. Enter the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn").

## Detailed Walkthrough

|  |
| --- |
| [Locations of the missing crests on a map of Castle Volkihar Courtyard](/wiki/File:SR-map-Castle_Volkihar_Courtyard.jpg "Locations of the missing crests on a map of Castle Volkihar Courtyard") [White pog.png](/wiki/File:White_pog.png)  Half  [White pog.png](/wiki/File:White_pog.png)  Full  [White pog.png](/wiki/File:White_pog.png)  Cres  Locations of the missing crests on a map of Castle Volkihar Courtyard |

[Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") will speak to you after the [Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") reads the Elder Scroll, saying she may know where to find one of the scrolls. She thinks her mother, [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica"), may have information on it, and may even possess it. Serana believes Valerica may have left a clue in the [courtyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Courtyard "Skyrim:Volkihar Courtyard") at [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar"). Though you will not be able to enter through the Keep, Serana knows of a secret entrance you can use. If you have a follower at this point, you must dismiss them. Simply telling them to wait is not enough: Serana won't accompany you unless you send your follower home.

When you reach the castle, head northwest, along the coastline. When you reach the castle's old docks, you will be attacked by four high-powered [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). Use the secret entrance to the [undercroft](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Undercroft "Skyrim:Volkihar Undercroft") and fight your way through [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), skeletons, and a [feral vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Feral_Vampire "Skyrim:Feral Vampire").

After dealing with the vampire, you will arrive at a stone archway with a raised drawbridge. Head up a set of stairs on the opposite corner of the room to find the lever needed to lower the bridge. Cross the bridge and take a left as instructed by Serana: this leads into an open area inhabited by death hounds. Climb the stairs in the southern section and pass through a tunnel leading to a room with a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider"). You can snipe at the spider from the tunnel, as it's too large to enter the tunnel. Once you've dispatched it, pull a lever to lower another bridge, giving you access to the courtyard.

The [courtyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Courtyard "Skyrim:Volkihar Courtyard") itself is abandoned and derelict, and Serana will immediately tell you there is something wrong with the moon dial. You will need to find the three missing pieces and place them in the moon dial in order for a secret entrance to open.

- The [Half Moon Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Half_Moon_Crest "Skyrim:Half Moon Crest") is in the center of a pond lying against a rock in the northwest corner of the courtyard.
- The [Full Moon Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Full_Moon_Crest "Skyrim:Full Moon Crest") is behind a patch of nightshade lying against the castle's exterior wall in the fenced off area identified as Valerica's garden.
- The [Crescent Moon Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescent_Moon_Crest "Skyrim:Crescent Moon Crest") is up the stairs, to the right of the entrance to [Volkihar North Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_North_Tower "Skyrim:Volkihar North Tower") lying on the floor beside a table and chairs.

Serana opening the portal to the Soul Cairn

Once all pieces are back in place, the dial will swivel to reveal steps leading down to the [ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Ruins "Skyrim:Volkihar Ruins") below the castle. Fight your way past more [gargoyles](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle") and skeletons until you reach a room with gargoyles and a fireplace. Serana will tell you there must be a secret entrance somewhere, and sure enough, you can either turn the candlestick near the fireplace or pull the chain behind the gargoyle to reveal a secret door. Note that pulling the chain will unleash the stone gargoyle. There is also a [vampire royal armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Royal_Armor "Skyrim:Vampire Royal Armor") near the shelf to the right.

Head through the secret door to [Valerica's study](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica%27s_Study "Skyrim:Valerica's Study"). Here you will need to search for her [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Valerica's Journal"), in the central bookcase west of where you entered. After Serana reads it, she will tell you to find certain ingredients in the laboratory:

- The [Finely Ground Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Finely_Ground_Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Finely Ground Bone Meal") is on the table by the entrance beneath the mammoth skull.
- The [Soul Gem Shards](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Shards "Skyrim:Soul Gem Shards") are on the first wardrobe up the stairs that lead east.
- The [Purified Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Purified_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Purified Void Salts") are on a shelf with other ingredients, near the farthest point of the raised area of the room, on the balcony above the entrance.

All of these items are in silver bowls, and will be added to your miscellaneous inventory when you pick them up, as they are considered quest items. Note that "regular" [bonemeal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemeal "Skyrim:Bonemeal"), [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment"), and [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") will not work.

Once you have all three, place them in the vessel in front of the portal, which Serana is typically standing next to. She will then add her blood to the mixture, opening a portal to the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn").

If you are vampire (whether by siding with the Volkihar or through "regular" infection when siding with the Dawnguard), you will be able to enter straight away. If you are not a vampire, you will suffer some health damage when attempting to use the portal. Serana will explain that to enter the Soul Cairn you must be "dead" and then give you a choice:

- Allow her to turn you into a [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord").
- Allow her to trap part of your soul in a soul gem.
  - This is the only way to enter the Soul Cairn without becoming a vampire and will add the [Weakened Soul](/wiki/Skyrim:Weakened_Soul "Skyrim:Weakened Soul") effect, which reduces your health, stamina, and magicka by 45 points (as well as their regeneration rates) while in the Soul Cairn ([click here](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death") or [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") for workarounds).

Choosing either will allow you to enter the Soul Cairn.

## Gallery

- 

  Half Moon Crest
- 

  Full Moon Crest
- 

  Crescent Moon Crest

## Notes

- Before entering the Cairn, you can exit the laboratory through a door in the southern corner. This leads to the *Castle Volkihar Balcony*, a small outside area from which you can fast-travel and then return to the Soul Cairn without having to traverse the castle ruins and courtyard again. A foot chest near the door also provides easy access to a container to stash loot while fast-travelling.
  - If you exit before deciding whether to be become a Vampire Lord or have your soul captured, Serana will remain in the study, even if you fast travel. This presents a small window of opportunity to acquire two followers: leave the castle grounds, recruit a follower and return. Though your new follower won't enter the Castle, they will not be dismissed, and once you complete [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death") they will continue following you, as will Serana. This allows you to have two followers for the rest of the game.
  - If playing on [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") (which disables fast travel), the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") Shout can allow the balcony exit to remain a shortcut outside by jumping off the ledge. Otherwise you'll have to backtrack through the dungeons to go back outside.
- Choosing to become a Vampire Lord and then returning to Fort Dawnguard will prompt [Florentius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius"), [Sorine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard"), or [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") to direct you to [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion"), thus beginning the quest [Rising at Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn"). Other Dawnguard members, including [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran"), will regard you with caution and disgust. You will not be able to use the Dawnguard's services until you cure yourself.
- While this quest or [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death") are active, you will be unable to dismiss Serana from your party. If you are on the Dawnguard side and a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"), it can be challenging to use Beast Form and have the Savage Feeding perk as Serana tends to raise corpses in battle. This prevents you from feeding unless you manage to feed on raised corpses after they die again but before they turn into a pile of ash.
- From the courtyard you have access to two more zones of the castle - the [east](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_East_Tower "Skyrim:Volkihar East Tower") and [north](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_North_Tower "Skyrim:Volkihar North Tower") towers - which contain further loot.
- Serana may repeat dialogue about her mother being on the other side of the portal if you should decide to leave the ruins before entering the portal.

## Bugs

- When asked to put the ingredients inside the vessel, they will be removed from your inventory, but the vessel will not be filled, and Serana will keep telling you to put the ingredients in, causing the quest to be unfinishable.
  -  It is possible to manually advance to the next stage of the quest by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and typing `setstage DLC1VQ04 75` .
  -  This can also be caused by multi-follower mods. Typing 'set playerfollowercount to 0' will let the quest continue normally. Once back out of the Soul Cairn set the value back to the number of followers you have.
- When asked to speak to Serana after putting the ingredients inside the vessel, speaking to Serana does not advance the quest.
  -  It is possible to manually advance to the next stage of the quest by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and typing `setstage DLC1VQ04 90`.
- Dead Thralls cannot enter the Volkihar Courtyard. Entering the Courtyard can cause the thrall(s) to vanish from the game after returning from the Soul Cairn. Kill and leave the bodies of the thrall(s) in a safe place before entering the Courtyard.
- When Serana asks for the journal, it might not be removed from your inventory.
  - It can be dropped or stored once you rescue her mother and return from the Soul Cairn.
- You may not be able to enter the Soul Cairn.
  -  Open the console and type `set DLC1VQ04SoulTrapped to 1`.
- It is possible to get stuck in a loop where Serana tries to turn you into a vampire if you had previously elected to become a vampire and then for some reason did not enter the Soul Cairn to advance the quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.6, addresses this issue. The script call that actually performs the bite has been moved from Stage 110 into the dialogue topic itself, which will run whether you'd done this portion before or not.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQ04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQ04`.

Chief Burguk

Burguk surrounded by wives

**Chief Burguk**, an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerOneHandedMaster "Skyrim:TrainerOneHandedMaster"), is the chief of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"), the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") south of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). He is the master [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") and can train you up to level 90. A bit of a braggart, he will [challenge you](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!") to a [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl") to prove he is superior.

Due to Orc tradition, Burguk has several wives, including forge-wife [Gharol](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol "Skyrim:Gharol"), hunts-wife [Arob](/wiki/Skyrim:Arob "Skyrim:Arob"), and his favored wife [Shel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shel "Skyrim:Shel"). While the first two wives merely act as symbolic marriages, Shel gets all the attention from the chief and is the one who gets to spend time with him when he sits outside [his longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Burguk's Longhouse") between 7am and 7pm, doing nothing but watch the other tribe members work. At 7pm he heads inside the house and enjoys a five-hour dinner surrounded by his wives and sons, until he finally goes to bed at midnight.

He wears an almost-complete set of leveled [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") (up to [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish") quality at level 25), including a cuirass, boots, gauntlets, and two shields. He wields a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") and carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Key to Burguk's Longhouse") to the longhouse, a pair of [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers"), and some [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Fight! Fight!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!")**: Prove your strength by wagering on a fist fight with another. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

His potential greetings are:

:   *"You speak to Burguk, chief of Dushnikh Yal."*
:   *"Need a poison for your hunting? My mother, [Murbul](/wiki/Skyrim:Murbul "Skyrim:Murbul"), knows several."*
:   *"You need steel? Speak to my forge-wife, Gharol."*
:   *"This stronghold respects strength, and strength alone."*

If you ask him about training, he shows his pride by telling you:

:   **I'd like to train in One-Handed weapons.**
:   *"You'll never compare to me, but I can try and teach you anyway."*

If you are low on money when you speak to him, he will comment:

:   *"You're short on coin."*

## Conversations

When the entire family spends quality time in the longhouse, it soon becomes apparent that polygamous relationships can be problematic, even if it is tradition:

**Shel**: *"My chief, Gharol threatens to have me work in the mines. You won't allow my pretty hands to dirty, will you?"*
**Burguk**: *"No, my wife. You have been given other gifts to please your chief than mine work. I will talk to Gharol and all will be well."*
**Shel**: *"Oh, thank you my chief!"*

**Burguk**: *"I saw you working the forge today, wife. Your muscles have grown strong from the metal shaping!"*
**Gharol**: *"Do they, my chief? Am I now favored enough to replace Shel by your side at the feast? Back your words with action!"*
**Burguk**: *"No more talk of Shel. As chief, I will do what I please, so point your fiery gaze to our enemies."*

Burguk will also occasionally seek out his mother for advice:

**Burguk**: *"Tell me, mother, does Malacath favor our stronghold?"*
**Murbul**: *"He is pleased. Ours is the strongest tribe in all the Reach."*

## Unused Dialogue

Chief Burguk has unused dialogue tied to a quest he was once meant to give you. This dialogue can only be found in the game's DialogueViews files, and not the Creation Kit.

:   **Anything I can do for the Stronghold?**
:   *"I finally have an idea that will make Shugurzbur a place to be feared. Have you heard of the [Briar-Hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart")*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*? Strange magic created by [Hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). I'm told that if you eat one, you gain the strength of ten Orcs. Bring me one. There is a nest nearby you can scavenge."*

:   **I've brought you a Briar-Heart *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*.**
:   *"Ugh. It looks sharp. Oh well, an idea is an idea. Tastes... chewy. Yuck. I've eaten real [hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart") better than this. Strange. I don't feel any stronger. I... I think I need to lie down. Oh, wait. Yes. For you. Here. The stronghold thanks you, outlander."*

## Notes

- As the unused dialogue above indicates, as well as multiple internal references confirm, the stronghold was originally named **Shugurzbur**, rather than Dushnikh Yal.
  - In addition, the internal names for the unused dialogue confirm that Burguk was originally named **Yashnag** instead.
  - While the unused quest is internally known as `FreeformShugurzburB`, its companion quest `FreeformShugurzburA` still appears in the final game, albeit slightly reworked, as the quest [Gharol's Message](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol%27s_Message "Skyrim:Gharol's Message").
  - It's unknown what Hagraven nest Burguk mentions in his dialogue, as none are found in a close proximity to the stronghold in the final game.
- According to the game's Relationship data, Chief Burguk is also the father of [Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk"), a bard with a bad reputation residing in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). They are also marked as [rivals](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition#Relationship_Rank "Skyrim:Disposition"), so you may [receive a letter](/wiki/Skyrim:An_enemy%27s_gratitude "Skyrim:An enemy's gratitude") from one of them as gratitude for killing the other.
  - In the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, Lurbuk is even referred to as "**Lurbuk gro-Dushnikh**". Indicating his stronghold of origin as Dushnikh Yal.

Chief Larak

**Chief Larak** is the [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerBlockMaster "Skyrim:TrainerBlockMaster") and chieftain of the [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur") [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds"). He is a master shield-bearer and can thus [train](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") you in the art of [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") up to skill level 90. As with many Orc chieftains, Larak will challenge you to a [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl") for the bet of 100 gold. He is the son of [Sharamph](/wiki/Skyrim:Sharamph "Skyrim:Sharamph"), brother of [Bagrak](/wiki/Skyrim:Bagrak "Skyrim:Bagrak"), father of [Borgakh the Steel Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgakh_the_Steel_Heart "Skyrim:Borgakh the Steel Heart") and [Olur](/wiki/Skyrim:Olur "Skyrim:Olur") and a husband to [Shuftharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Shuftharz "Skyrim:Shuftharz").

He wears [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor") with a pair of [Forsworn boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Boots "Skyrim:Forsworn Boots") and is armed with a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") that may both be up to [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish") in quality. He also carries a pair of [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers"), the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Key to Larak's Longhouse") to [Larak's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Larak's Longhouse") and [a selection of common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Fight! Fight!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!")**: Prove your strength by wagering on a fist fight with another. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

:   *"You are speaking to Larak, chief of Mor Khazgur."*
:   *"You should see my forge-wife, Shuftharz, if you need weapons or armor."*
:   *"My mother, Sharamph, knows many remedies you may wish to take with you."*
:   *"My place is chief and my challenge is to lead my people."*
:   *"I'm a strict follower of the old traditions. Honor, strength, deeds."*

If you elect to train with him, he will remark:

:   *"You wish to learn from the best, eh? So be it."*

As he is a chieftain he can be asked about some of the [Orc traditions](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Orc_Strongholds_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue"). He shares the following dialogue with all other chiefs:

:   **You're the chief?**
:   *"Yes. I earned the right by slaying my father in single combat. One day, I will have a son who will challenge me when I become too old to lead, and the stronghold will have a new chief. Until then, I alone have the right to have wives and children. It ensures our strength."*

:   **How do the Orcs govern themselves?**
:   *"The Code of [Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:Malacath "Skyrim:Malacath"). It is both tradition and law in the strongholds. Break the code, and you must pay Blood Price. The code is not written anywhere. It is known and carried on by the Orcs, and all who live in the strongholds follow it. For an outlander, following it is simple. Do not steal or attack anyone in the stronghold, or be ready to pay in gold or blood."*

:   **Are there other strongholds out there?**
:   *"There are a few great strongholds worthy to talk about. Dushnikh Yal, Mor Khazgur, Narzulbur, and Largashbur."*

### Conversations

Larak may be seen having random conversations with his mother or his son:

:   **Sharamph**: *"Malacath is pleased with your strength, Larak."*
:   **Larak**: *"I am honored."*

:   **Larak**: *"The way you and your mother forge weapons is impressive.*"
:   **Olur**: *"It's simple Orc smithing practice, my chief. Nothing that hasn't been passed down for years."*
:   **Larak**: *"I served in the Legion. Perhaps I'll show you some of their technique one of these days."*

:   **Larak**: *"Your muscles ripple when you work the forge. It's pleasing."*
:   **Shuftharz**: *"Thank you, my chief."*

## Unused Dialogue

Chief Larak has unused dialogue tied to a quest he was once meant to give you. This dialogue can only be found in the game's DialogueViews files, and not the Creation Kit. He would've given you the task of picking up some special bracers made by [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). Although the dialogue for starting the quest no longer seems to exist, the ending portion does remain.

:   **I have your bracers from Ghorza.**
:   *"Good. The craft is as good as any stronghold smith. You have done well. Here, take my bow in trade for your help."*

## Notes

- The game data notes Larak as `InLawParent` and not as `Parent` to both Borgakh and Olur, making it possible that Larak took in Borgakh and Olur as his own children.
- The game data marks Bagrak as a spouse to Larak, yet both Larak and Bagrak refer to Sharamph as their mother. Given that Orc women are married off to other strongholds, it does seem strange that Bagrak would remain at Mor Khazgur if she is to be Larak's sister.
- His wife, Shuftharz, may mention her support for her husband, saying *"The forge is strong and so is our chief, Larak. I'm content."* Larak's sister Bagrak, however, seems to think he has not quite reached his full potential as chief yet, saying *"Larak is strong, but he has much to prove as chief."*

## Bugs

- Sometimes when he is sitting in the chair outside the longhouse, he does not interact with anything.
- He may not brawl you.
  - This may be fixed by entering then exiting a building and trying again.

## Overview

Chief Mauhulakh

**Chief Mauhulakh** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardOrc2H "Skyrim:GuardOrc2H") and Chieftain of [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur"), the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). His stronghold runs the [Gloombound Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloombound_Mine "Skyrim:Gloombound Mine"), which is rich in [ebony ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore"). If asked for available work, he will [challenge you](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!") to a [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl").

Mauhulakh sits outside his [longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Mauhulakh%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Mauhulakh's Longhouse") from 7am to 7pm, when he goes inside to eat with his family until midnight.

He spends his days wondering why the gods are angry with him. As an Orc chieftain, he should have multiple wives, but he has none. Every wife he has taken has died soon after, several during childbirth, including the mothers of his son, [Dushnamub](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnamub "Skyrim:Dushnamub"), and daughter, [Urog](/wiki/Skyrim:Urog "Skyrim:Urog"). Four graves can be found, up a hill behind the longhouse. Despite his predicament, he is still friendly towards outsiders. While he waits for a wife worthy of the gods, he is taken care of by his two aunts, [Bolar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolar "Skyrim:Bolar") and [Yatul](/wiki/Skyrim:Yatul "Skyrim:Yatul"), a strange relationship that hasn't gone unnoticed by his son. Although they cannot provide him what he wants, more children. Making him look weak even further is the fact that he had to hire outsiders from another tribe to work in the mine to make up for the lack of native tribesmen.

## Related Quests

- **[Fight! Fight!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!")**: Prove your strength by wagering on a fist fight with another. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"The blessings of the mine have been many, but I have no mate to share them."*
:   *"Been married many times but the gods keep taking them from me."*
:   *"The great stronghold of Narzulbur welcomes you, outsider."*
:   *"Come to purchase ebony? Our Gloombound Mine runs thick with black veins."*

## Conversations

As the stronghold's chief, Mauhulakh will often have conversations with his family:

**Mauhulakh**: *"Bolar, I must ask you something."*
**Bolar**: *"Yes, child?"*
**Mauhulakh**: *"Have the spirits told you where I may find a wife? One who will be safe from this curse?"*
**Bolar**: *"Oh, all things in time, my boy. All things in time. What more do you need that Yatul and I cannot provide?"*
**Mauhulakh**: *"I need more children."*
**Bolar**: *"Well, that's a different matter..."*

**Mauhulakh**: *"Are the gods angry with me?"*
**Bolar**: *"Why do you ask me that?"*
**Mauhulakh**: *"Why else have they cursed me? Killed all my wives?"*
**Bolar**: *"Perhaps it's actually a sign of their love for you. They don't want to see you with unworthy mates."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"Then they should send one they consider worthy."*
**Bolar**: *"Patience, boy."*

**Mauhulakh**: *"You wanted to see me?"*
**Yatul**: *"Bolar said you had been looking for a new wife?"*
**Mauhulakh**: *"Well, I..."*
**Yatul**: *"I don't think you're quite ready yet."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"How will I know when I'm ready?"*
**Yatul**: *"Bolar and I will tell you."*

**Mauhulakh**: *"Bolar has been in a bad mood for weeks, now."*
**Yatul**: *"Oh? I hadn't noticed."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"Since Galka was taken from us. She's been... sad, I guess."*
**Yatul**: *"She's just worried about you. We all are. We just want you to be happy. We want to make you happy."*

**Mauhulakh**: *"How is your hunting with Yatul?"*
**Urog**: *"We are strong. We get the job done."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"I'm proud of you for helping provide for us."*
**Urog**: *"Well someone has to provide around here."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"What is that supposed to mean?"*
**Urog**: *"Nothing."*

**Mauhulakh**: *"I don't know what your aunts told you, but..."*
**Urog**: *"They're not my aunts. They're your aunts. And they told me enough."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"What are you talking about?"*
**Urog**: *"About how the Divines cursed you. What horrible thing did you do to deserve it?"*
**Mauhulakh**: *"Nothing! I... it's ill fortune. That's all."*
**Urog**: *"Well, your ill fortune means I have no mother."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"I... I'm sorry."*

**Mauhulakh**: *"Haven't I always been a good father? A good chief?"*
**Urog**: *"Yatul and I do all the hunting. [Mul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mul_gro-Largash "Skyrim:Mul gro-Largash") and [Gadba](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadba_gro-Largash "Skyrim:Gadba gro-Largash") do all the mining. It seems like all you do is find more wives to get killed."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"That's not fair, now."*
**Urog**: *"Just... try and keep out of our way."*

**Dushnamub**: *"Don't you ever wonder, father?"*
**Mauhulakh**: *"All the time."*
**Dushnamub**: *"But your aunts don't even seem to care."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"They are good women. They love me. You will speak no more ill of them."*
**Dushnamub**: *"I've just never heard of a midwife losing all her mothers like that."*

**Dushnamub**: *"Father, I'm worried about Gadba and Mul."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"What about them?"*
**Dushnamub**: *"You don't worry about two Orc men coming into your stronghold? That they might challenge you?"*
**Mauhulakh**: *"They're miners. Harmless."*
**Dushnamub**: *"I've just learned not to trust luck around here."*

**Mauhulakh**: *"Someday, you can have your own stronghold."*
**Dushnamub**: *"I think it may have to be far away from here."*
**Mauhulakh**: *"Oh, if you're worried about me trying to meddle with you..."*
**Dushnamub**: *"It's not you I'm worried about."*

## Unused Dialogue

Mauhulakh was once intended to give you a quest, which only has the internal name `NarzulburFreeFormWifeQuest` left. While your responses seem to be missing, all of Mauhulakh's lines seem to be intact.

:   *"The mine is rich, and so are we. But I am cursed, it would seem, to live alone."*

:   *"I've had several wives. But each dies sooner than the last. I was lucky to get children out of the ones I did."*

:   *"Everyone said it had run out, but I smashed down one wall and found the widest veins of ebony I'd ever seen. So now we're rich and now I'm chief."*

:   *"I think of [Uglarz](/wiki/Skyrim:Uglarz "Skyrim:Uglarz"). An old friend. When we were little she ran to the woods to hunt, and never came back. If someone found her, she would make an excellent mate."*

:   *"Ha. Good luck to you, friend. She's not one who likes to be found."*

Once Uglarz was found and brought to the stronghold, Mauhulakh could now greet you by saying:

:   *"I'm hoping this wife can outlast the winter."*

## Notes

- The outfit that Chief Mauhulakh wears is actually known as `DEMO_ArmorScaledHelmetOutfit` internally. It was originally used for an Imperial bandit related to a demo, as its name implicates.
